Ardul

Lt. Ardul is the right-hand officer for Captain Xulleyl. He is her trusted advisor in all things, and makes sure that everyone else knows that he is her favorite. His sneer and superiority elicit easy loathing.

  • - Trynn's observation -

A self-satisfied little sycophant, that's what he is.

-Zacxh's-

Cousin to The inept and *new* forman of the mines.

Stole the Rubies for unknown purpose and fenced them through unknown channels.

Had/has at least one mine spy in his guard unit (Jhull)

does not like me.

last edited 2006-01-30 03:30:43 by Cliff

Arts

Dark elves have a rich culture, filled with aesthetic crafts and arts. It is expected that all Dark Elves will become skilled in at least one craft or art and contribute creations or skills to the betterment of their house and/or city.

Dance of the Scorching Beauty

Hit die

d6

Requirements

Perform: 8 ranks Tumble: 8 Ranks

Class Skills

Appraise (Int), Balance (Dex), Bluff (Cha), Climb (Str), Concentration (Con), Craft (Int), Decipher Script (Int), Diplomacy (Cha), Disguise (Cha), Escape Artist (Dex), Gather Information (Cha), Hide (Dex), Jump (Str), Knowledge (all skills, taken individually) (Int), Listen (Wis), Move Silently (Dex), Perform (Cha), Profession (Wis), Sense Motive (Wis), Sleight of Hand (Dex), Speak Language (None), Spellcraft (Int), Swim (Str), Tumble (Dex), and Use Magic Device (Cha).

Skill Points at Each Level

6 + Int modifier.

Class Features

Weapon and armor proficiency

The Bellydancer is proficient with all simple weapons, the scimitar, the finger cymbals, and the scarf.

+1 Existing casters level

For every level of belly dancer the belly dancer gains an additionally level in the spellcasting ability of one spellcasting class she had before becoming a belly dancer.

Tools of the trade

The scimitar, finger cymbals, and scarf become useful as performance equipment and battle weapons at first level. The Belly dancer is able to seductively dance and battle with her weapons simultaneously. The scimitar is used as a slashing weapon as are the finger cymbals (d4 damage, crit on 19-20). The scarf is useful as a five foot range disarming and tripping weapons with +2 to that task (an additional +4 if the belly dancer can beat her opponent in a contest of her perform versus their sense motive). and doesn’t draw an attack of opportunity. Furthermore a the belly dancer moves as a seductive and graceful dance for all of combat all of these weapons usages are not only instantly interchangeable (no need for an action for drawing a weapon), but seductive and alluring to boot.

Moves of the Trade

At second level the belly dancer has mastered being charming on stage and off. This gives their performances, spells, and all other action a level of charisma they didn’t have before. At level 2 the belly dancer gains the Alluring feat.

Armor of Cuteness

No warrior can stand against the belly dancer’s secret weapon, her smile. At third level this gives the belly dancer the ability to play upon this reluctance in combat, giving her a miscellaneous bonus to AC equal to her charisma bonus.

Dance magic

At fourth level the belly dancer’s spellcasting and performance ability merge. The dances of the belly dancer seem to become magical themselves, giving her a +2 innate modifier for perform checks, and giving her the disguise spell feat.

Gypsy Band

At fifth level the belly dancer has become such a performer that she attracts others to her cause, forming a roving band of gypsies, thieves, and musicians to serve as her companions, band, and fellow performers. The attracted followers may be of ill repute, but will fall within one adjustment of the belly dancer’s alignment, making them perhaps lovable scoundrels. Treat as Leadership, but without the advantage of a cohort.

Armor of Grace

No warrior’s sword can match the swift and graceful motions of a belly dancer’s most dangerous weapons, her hips. At level six the belly dancer has refined her combat dancing to the point where she can dodge, evade, and avoid attacks without breaking her all important rhythm. The belly dancing bard gains a dodge bonus to AC equal to her dexterity bonus.

Dance of the scimitars

At level 8 the belly dancer has mastered a traditional dance known by all master belly dancers, the dance of the scimitars. In this dance the belly dancer balances scimitars on various parts of her body to the amazement and chagrin of her enemies. To perform this dance the belly dancer must succeed in a DC 20 perform check and have two scimitars (or other bladed weapons of similar design [short swords, long swords all styled as scimitars). While performing this dance, the belly dancer fights with the two blades as if she had ambidexterity and two weapons fighting, but maintains a suitable amount of stylized combat sex-appeal.

Dance of the Alluring Blossom

At level 9 the bellydancer masters another dance. This dance woos her audience with its irresistible beat and seductive movements of the body. The bellydancer makes a perform check while doing this dance. All who look upon her must make a will save equal to half of the perform check result or be held fascinated for as long as the bellydancer continues to dance (this dance requires the bellydancer to exclusively do only this dance for the duration). Those who succeed the will save are dazed for one round as they take in her Beauty for just a moment before breaking its hold. This dance can be done once per day.

Dance of the Scorching Beauty

At level 10 the bellydancer has developed such an ability of merging high-speed hip movement into magical enticements she has mastered yet another dance. Like the supernaturally beautiful nymph the bellydancer can summon more beauty than mere mortals can behold. Once per day the bellydancer can perform a dance, the Dance of the scorching beauty, that will cause onlookers to die or go blind. To perform this dance the bellydancer makes a perform check. All people looking upon her at the time must make a fort save equal to half of that perform check or die. Those who save are blinded for 4d6 rounds.

Ruthless pillaged from http://www.eralston.com/downloads/Bellydancer.doc

last edited 2006-03-22 22:18:39 by Barrett

Bhaerynden

Lucrative goldmine and waypoint on the way from both Nerr'tenden and T'lethtyrr to Dolthgurdar. Outpost of House Keniryn and post of Illiam. Until recently traffic from Bhaerynden had been plagued by marauders in the catacombs separating it from Llurth Dreier. Caravan traffic has seemingly returned to normal, though several conspicuous non-merchant parties from Dolthgurdar have passed through on their way to Nerr'tenden in recent weeks.

last edited 2007-03-19 21:58:20 by Andrew

Catacomb Bandits

Band of toughs hiding out in the Catacombs between Bhaerynden and Llurth Dreier responsible for attacking several caravans bound for Dolthgurdar. According to Sharb, they were conscripted by Flikk under orders from House Orlylyl. Bhaerynden gold recovered from their hideout was melted down and used to finance their employment with House Oussund in Nerr'tenden after their defeat by the Spider Guard and recruitment by Nal. The circumstances of their loyalty to Nal remain a mystery. The Spider Guard assisted the bandits in making it easy for Orlylyl to believe they had been completely routed by ransacking the bandits' hideout but leaving a stash of House Godendar rubies for their former masters to find.

last edited 2007-03-18 19:42:22 by Andrew

ChapterEight

Chapter Eight: Insanity, Mages and Intrigue, as the quest for a good bottle of wine continues.

He did not have to wait long. He scouted around the main chamber of Nerr’tenden looking for a nice sniper roost. The 'ceiling' of the place reached up well out of sight. hundreds of feet at least. Zacxh wondered where the giant tapering chimney terminated. Someday he would climb up there and explore.

His circular route took him near the post where Anthadax the distracted Oussund mage was pacing furiously. Zacxh paused a moment wondering if he should press his luck by speaking to the mercurial wizard then approached.

'Sir, may I speak?' Zacxh was strangely drawn to this reclusive and extremely powerful elf.

'Do as you like but be quick.' Zacxh covertly looked the wizard over and saw that he was covered in ceremonial scarring. Minor wounds were scabbing all over his arms. This Ossund mage, like so many others who habitually exposed themselves to the arcane, was clearly insane. The elf seemed an unnatural blend of ability and perverse self destructiveness. To watch him was to glimpse a barely functional lunatic, always at the brink of unleashing some horrific and rare force of nature.

Some would argue that arcana, by its very definition was unnatural. Zacxh did not agree. He had seen many 'unnatural' forces manifest them self through the mere power of his concentration. He felt that arcana was merely a word for those special aspects of 'nature' which only revealed them self under rare and special circumstances.

Anthadax had clearly sacrificed large tracts of his soul in the exploration of those circumstances.

'Sir I hope to position myself so as to ambush any attackers which present themselves. Where should I hide so as to avoid being broiled alive by your magics?'

The mage did not look at Zacxh as he spoke, and his voice was disinterested and distracted.

'I will focus on troop concentrations and the most dangerous enemies first. stay away from those.'

Zacxh could see that Anthadax was done speaking and though interested in trying to draw the elf out a bit, he bowed and moved off.

Zacxh circled around a bit more and found a nice little ledge about sixty feet up the wall. He closed his eyes a moment and focused himself, then ran at the wall and impossibly ran right up to the perch. Unnatural...

He pulled out and strung his heavy bow then loosened a few arrows in his quiver. Satisfied all was ready, he crossed his legs sat down to wait. Soon Sorn walked up the wall and sat down next to him. If Zacxh had momentarily bent the laws of gravity and momentum to attain the perch, Sorn openly defied them.

Sorn sat down next to Zacxh at a right angle to the floor and started in.

'You and I haven't spoken since the incident with Kadyel.'

Zacxh immediately grew a bit annoyed at having to again defend his actions and responded coolly.

'Incident? Oh, you must mean when I killed her for being a dangerous and insipid traitor... What is it you would like to say about it?'

Zacxh thought that would kill the conversation, but Sorn pressed on.

'Yeah well I don't miss her, but just because we didn't like her doesn't mean you had the right to kill her. I came here to better my life. I see the Spiderguard as a means of increasing my station and bettering my life. I was happy before I came here and thought this was a place where I could find great opportunity. Now that you killed Kadyel I fear for my life and wonder if I might not be next.'

Zacxh had little patience for this inquisition, but could not help but feel an urge to be understood by this nieve young elf. Perhaps he felt as if Sorn represented part of the conscience which he lost so long ago in the secret fighting arena of house Ossund.

'Look Sorn, I am a practical elf who prefers actions to arguments. Kadyel was a real and pressing threat to not just me but to all of us. You may not like it that I killed her, but someday you will realize that by doing so, I probably saved your life. Or, maybe I am wrong. Either way, I sleep better at night not looking over my shoulder for her next attack, and that alone makes the whole thing worthwhile.'

'You have little enough to fear from me. In fact, if you only knew what an act of absolute loyalty to you my execution of Kadyel was, you would be looking at me as a dear friend not like one of the heads of Valron's mother's whip.'

Sorn was a bit taken aback.

'You use this word friend, and you speak often of loyalty. I am unfamiliar with these things...'

Zacxh let a rare grin surface upon his otherwise empty face.

'Well I have searched into the meaning of these things many years now. Certainly, I am no expert, merely an apprentice practitioner of the art, but I have great confidence that if we are to survive, we will all soon have to show good measures of each. I feel that these ideas are especially critical for warriors and those who rely upon each other for their survival. Without loyalty and friends who were willing to sacrifice for me (as I have sacrificed for you) I would have died a lonely and anonymous death ages ago in the pits. In fact, of all the weapons available to me in a fight, I figure the loyalty of my comrades is by far the most important. That is why I fight so fearlessly in defense of the Spiderguard and *that*, above all else, is ultimately why Kadyel had to die.'

Zacxh could see Sorn working on this idea and decided to back away from the topic to give his young friend time to ponder it.

'So Sorn, How do you find the food here? Personally, I find it horrible. For a while I was overwhelmed by the copious quantities and easy access of the stuff, but of late those aspects of the vile slop only accentuate how truly repulsive it is.'

Sorn looked at Zacxh anew.

'Maybe there is more to you than I thought...'

The discussion turned to food and wine and other fine things, and at last the two elves found some common ground. Zacxh told Sorn of his decision to stop eating anything that failed to nourish the spirit as well as the body. Then asked that the refined elf let him know if he came across anything particularly worth tasting. They also joked about bedding Inarra and other companionable things. Minutes stretched to hours which they passed comfortably.

After awhile, Zacxh decided to get some rest while waiting for the fight to begin. He forced his mind to bend its perceptions of time and space and ran down the wall. Sorn only smiled at how difficult Zacxh made it look. At the bottom Zacxh folded himself up and without ceremony, drifted into a restful trance.

He started to alertness several hours later. Nothing moved, yet something was different. He felt refreshed as he stretched He must have dozed for several hours. Soon a messenger ran through the front gait toward the armory. Zacxh stirred his rested body to its feet and soon Captain Xulleyl emerged walking toward him.

'It begins' she said 'Go get the others.'

Zacxh nodded to his Captain then ran full speed to the common room, unconsciously sprinting up walls to speed his navigation of corners. Walls became floors and low ceilings which he ducked and dodged in his mad flight. His body came more and more alive with each moment of his ballistic exertion. By the time he came skidding to the door of the barracks, he was limbered up and again ready for the coming battle.

He stepped in quickly told Nal and Valron, who happened to be by the door to the commons, that the fight was about to start. Without pause for questions, Zacxh spun on his heel returned at a sprint to Sorn and the sniper's roost.

Zacxh strung his new bow and admired its craftsmanship. Few would have the strength to fully draw the stout weapon, Sorn might not be able to bend it at all, but Zacxh knew it was well matched to his strength and though difficult and tiring to wield, it would provide impressive results. He notched an arrow and waited.

Four strangers entered bearing a dead elf on a stretcher. They set it down and looked about nervously. Then one spoke.

'This Ossund spy was caught amongst the court of house Orlylyl. He bears the mark and manner of a Nerr’tenden spy. House Orlylyl hereby declares war!'

Zacxh was taken aback by the proclamation a moment. What spy did Xulleyl have who might be caught? Why announce the attack so, and what was it about this spy that was so offensive as to precipitate war. Suddenly is was clear. The lowly looking servants were more than mere messengers. They were trusted scouts, probably quite skilled, who came to assess the state of affairs here inside Nerr’tenden before beginning the raid.

The Orlylyl speaker reached into his pocket and drew out a small orb. Zacxh knew he should fire and kill the crier before he could deploy the thing, but almost as if entranced, he watched. The scout tossed the orb into the air where it floated up and split into four with a strange pop. The faintly glowing balls began to hum and just as Zacxh instinctively winced, they let out a horribly bright and blinding flash. Each orb started flashing and humming. The great chamber became a painfully brilliant, strobing scene of chaos. Fighters, both Ossund and Orlylyl appeared on all quadrants and engaged throughout the room.

Zacxh spied the crier enchanting powerful entanglement spells. Zacxh took aim and fired an arrow at him. He dared not look too long through his squinted eyes to see the effect of his shot but he did hear a satisfying meaty thud and a bit off cry of pain as the arrow found its mark. Sadly, the cry did not sound fatal, so Zacxh fired again. Another cry, though the meat cleaving sound of the arrow slamming home was drowned out by the whoosh of a strange fire spell detonating near the great room entrance.

Zacxh squinted over and saw that everything within thirty paces or so of the entrance was on fire. The spy body, the stone, several combatants, all of it. Zacxh fired at another combatant, but a strobe of light thwarted his view of the arrows effect and caused his vision to become little more than one great orange spot. He heard the arrow strike stone.

'Damn those lights, I can barely see!'

Nearby, Sorn was faring worse. The levitating elf curled himself into a defensive ball and clutched his head in his hands.

'Zacxh what is happening, I can't see a thing. I am blinded...'

Zacxh grinned at the blinking elf and drew another arrow.

'We are safe enough here young warrior. Give it a few moments and I believe your eyes will recover. I will stay nearby until you can see.'

Zacxh spotted another target surging and lurching in strobe lit motion. He squinted his eyes nearly closed to avoid the painful flashing light and aimed toward the center of his targets blurry motions. His arrow was surreally illuminated in flight by two nearly simultaneous flashes and in the following moment he watched a wizard lurch under the impact of the shot. The arrow pinned the dying mage's elbow to his ribcage and the Orlylyl wizard collapsed with a gurgled cry of pain.

Zacxh saw Trynn and Valron moving about below him and it looked as if Valron had fatally skewered at least one foe and stood boldly awaiting another. Valron's rigid stance and sweeping trident motions made it clear that he was as blind as Sorn. Zacxh looked too long at his friend and leader and forgot to squeeze his eyes shut at the sound of an impending 'pop' of light. He was dazzled a moment. Almost blinded. The heroic pose of Valron brandishing his trident at unseen foes momentarily hovered in his retinas as a glowing wavering orange and blue shifting afterimage.

Zacxh drew an arrow, heaved back with all his might and fired blindly with his eyes squeezed tight toward the main gate. He thought he had seen motion there a moment ago. He strained his hearing for a meaty sounding impact but perceived nothing in the riotous chaos. He froze a moment in mid draw to throw open some of the doors of his mental fortress. He felt his body stiffen as the demons of his past began to take hold of his physical form. He felt the cold detachment return, and fearing for his sanity lest he end up like Anthadax, quickly took refuge deep within himself, far away from anyplace he was likely to encounter the horrors which began to gleefully run the corridors of his mind.

He fired his bow again, only slightly noticing that it felt like the toy bow of a child in his rage powered arms. The arrow flew toward the main gates and he was sure he hared a grunt of pain about the time it should have found a mark.

Just then a powerful female voice, undoubtedly that of a priestess, rang forth from the gate.

'APPROACH!'

Somehow Zacxh knew instinctively the command was meant for someone else. He looked about and saw Captain Xulleyl running mindlessly toward the voice.

'Sorn, you are okay here. Stay put, and I will come back for you in a minute.'

Sorn blinked again. His vision seemed to be improving. 'No I'm okay. You go. I will fend for myself.'

Zacxh dropped his bow safe on the tiny perch and half ran, half fell down the wall into the melee below. His body was full under the sway of inner horrors now and he found himself drawing his blade and charging into the flames toward the source of that dreadful voice. He knew he would not survive long in the inferno of Anthadax's fire spell, but though he smelled his flesh and clothing burn, as yet he felt no pain.

Deep inside his mental fortress, secluded from the pain and immediacy of the battle, Zacxh wondered if Anthadax's firestorm was a dryly humored response to Zacxh's comment about being broiled alive. He doubted it, the mage seemed too distracted and self absorbed to give much though or care to anything said by a former slave. Still...

The fires raged much hotter than Zacxh had imagined possible. His scars stood up purple and angry and seemed to harden against the fire. It was not enough.

A few more strides and he drew up beside Trynn, Xulleyl, and a large and terrifying Priestess. Behind her were a dozen or so of what Zacxh assumed to be the warrior elite of Orlylyl. Xulleyl and an enlarged Trynn were dancing and lunging around the priestess. They did not appear to be having much success.

Zacxh decided to attack one of the Warriors. The heavily armed elf seemed surprised to see Zacxh emerge from the bright flames and greasy smoke and even more surprised when Zacxh's sword plunged toward his heart. The Warrior twisted painfully away reducing the effect of Zacxh's stroke, but was none the less badly wounded. He panicked and tried to wheel away and Zacxh swiped at him again laying open the flesh covering his left leg.

Zacxh turned from the fleeing fighter to face off against the terrifying Priestess. She radiated power and rage, and her presence on the battlefield was nearly overwhelming. She must have been wreathed in some sort of enchantment. He fought back an uncharacteristic surge of panic at the sight of her. The flames were beginning to overwhelm his flesh and he knew he could not spend much more time within the inferno Anthadax had wrought. If only Trynn could pin her a bit, Zacxh might be able to slip his blade into the Lolth Daughter's neck and silence her dire tongue as he had so recently silenced Kadyel’s.

Trynn groped his huge arms at her again and Xulleyl plunged a dagger into her side but Trynn's grasp was dodged even as a snake headed whip bit into his flesh. Trynn wailed in horror, then turned and fled.

Zacxh understood. He had faced those whips time and again. The venom of them caused panic and pain. Zacxh had tried to flee in terror before their wrath many times himself.

Zacxh assessed the situation. Xulleyl had obviously regained herself and seemed unaffected by the flames. His rescue of the Captain unnecessary, It was time for Zacxh to go. His chance to chop out the heart of the vile priestess would have to wait. He would fall back from this losing tactic and figure out a new vector of attack. Maybe the wizard would soften the Lolth bitch up a bit before Zacxh reengaged.

Valron's matron looked Zacxh square in the eye and issued another command.

'FLEE!' It was not a request.

Zacxh nearly laughed at the nerve of that witch to issue him orders when the enchantment took hold. At first Zacxh felt at though he was being motivated by one of the many demons he had released within his mind. Then he understood. He was bewitched.

His body was running at a full sprint directly away from the Priestess of Lolth. One of the ghosts rampaging about Zacxh's battle giddy mind found something tremendously funny about the whole situation.

He laughed demonically as he ran. 'Mutiny!'

Zacxh cleared the flames and drew up to the far wall of the cavern when the madness passed. He filled with hate and looked around.

Trynn stood nearby looking terrorized.

Anthadax had apparently vaporized several foes with some sort of acrid smelling energy and had caused others to simply detonate into bloody, stumpy, wiggling piles of gore. Zacxh watched the twisted mage a moment as he watched over a helpless victim of one of his spells who was writhing in agony and screaming horribly. It was a bit disturbing not to mention very loud. Zacxh walked up with a sword to deliver a death stroke to the wracked wizard but Anthadax stopped him.

'Leave him.' Again, not a request.

Zacxh shrugged and turned toward the flames. He steeled himself for another charge when Xulleyl and Valron's matron emerged. It appeared they had reached some sort of a truce.

Valron strode up indignant and started demanding explanations. He told of the dead and marked spy that the Spiderguard had found and suggested that a joint Ossund and Orlylyl investigation uncover who was trying to turn the two houses against each other.

Politics and intrigue. Zacxh quickly lost interest. Let the women and nobles sort this out amongst themselves. Zacxh would involve himself in practical matters.

He turned his attention to salvaging equipment and piling it into neat stacks. He wandered about the blood strewn and smoking battlefield picking over the bodies of the dead and keeping a watch on the Orlylyl warriors who were still hovering just outside the main gates.

He finished his salvage all the while serenaded by the anguished screams of Anthadax’s tormented victim then walked over and stood square in the middle of the entrance to face off Orlylyl's warrior detachment. Several Orlylyl sneered at the Idea of Zacxh standing a solo watch against their many. The soldier nursing his nasty chest and leg wound was not one of those. Zacxh stared each down coolly with his dripping sword held loosely in practiced hands. Soon the sneers stopped and Zacxh felt their confidence waver.

Lt. Ardul arrived after a time with his guard. Zacxh was struck as always by the faith Xulleyl placed in her suspicious lieutenant and without a word, he surrendered his vigil to wander toward the bath house. Valron, Nal and Xulleyl would doubtless be busy with their guest awhile and Zacxh had weapons to clean. His skin was tender from flames that would have killed any of those currently standing watch at the gate and he could use a soak.

Zacxh pitied the rest of the Spiderguard their interest in the two faced lies and bluffs which were about to transpire between houses Orlylyl and Ossund. Long experience with priestesses had taught him there would be nothing but poison and death in her words. Zacxh nearly thanked Lolth he was spared the audience, then realized that Lolth had nothing to do with it, or at least nothing to do with him. Zacxh was an elf without faith in the bloated spider queen. He knew she only provided agony and suffering. Never strength, at least not to the likes of himself. The elves of the Underdark had bent to her will for countless millennia. She was the source of their power but also of their limitations. Zacxh seethed in hatred of the Spider Queen a moment as he had so often before then noticed Anthadax still tormenting his screaming pet.

Zacxh took in the scene anew. Anthadax's bleeding arms and gore laced nails suddenly failed to impress Zacxh. Here was just another insane victim of The Spider Queen. Despite all his arcane power, he had lost himself. Too driven for power. Motivated only to achieve greater influence and security in this poisonous twisted world, the poor foolish noble had driven himself mad.

Zacxh grimaced. Such a waste. All that potential squandered when Anthadax could have lived as a king. The sadistic mage could have used his noble status and tremendous arcane power to actually enjoy his life. Instead there he stood mindlessly extracting horror and anguish from some helpless wretch. Did he even hear the screams? Did the sight of all that misery stir some memory of what it was once like to feel?

As he quietly strode past the scene toward the bath house, Anthadax's twisted state deeply touched Zacxh's sense of tragedy.

There was much wrong with the world that no amount of wine would dull, and no bar of soap would cleanse. The only cure lay somewhere within himself. Zacxh felt it with rare certainty. The question was where or what or how.

Only the insane could be oblivious to the insanity of their world. Maybe Anthadax had it right after all. Perhaps the only path to happiness lay in letting mind and conscious destroy itself. Zacxh resolved to meditate on that further while soaking.

Anthadax had his obsessions and Zacxh had his own. At least Zacxh's left him smelling nice. Perhaps tomorrow he would enlist Sorn's help in finding a decent bottle of wine.

last edited 2006-06-12 17:28:00 by Cliff

ChapterEleven

Chapter Eleven The bag.

Saner minds prevailed and the party rested for a few hours in the Mind flayer's lair. Zacxh normally would have volunteered for the first watch, but his head was pounding and his body ached in every joint. He was so mentally and emotionally exhausted by the furious mental battle he had fought with the mind flayers that he found himself slumping heavily on the ground and insensible in a restful trance before the rest of the party had even finished sorting out their gear from the fight. Zacxh was, as usual, physically uninjured by the battle, but his mind and spirit were ravaged. He had for the first time in memory found the absolute limit of his mental reserves. He sought his mental fortress to escape the ache in his bones but it was collapsed by fatigue. Zacxh had never experienced anything like it.

He woke from his dreamless trance to Inarra's voice as she plyingly discussed some matter of strategy with Nal. The day was in full bloom and the walls radiated a reassuringly warm glow. The radiance illuminated the lair in stark relief and Zacxh could see clearly his surroundings. The Lair... it all came back in a flash. The battle, his fatigue, all of it returned like a recollection from childhood. Well rested, Zacxh saw the incident as a cautionary yet somehow distant event. Don't underestimate the Illithid. They are deadly.

The Spiderguard formed up into their accustomed positions and moved out. Zacxh took point with Sorn and moved out to just within eyeshot. Zacxh practiced his silent movement but was nowhere as proficient in the art as the dancer with his nimble feet and absolute balance. Sorn could all but disappear at will, and Zacxh suspected that there was a bit more to it than mere stealth. The eerie little elf sometimes appeared to actually vanish when he was trying to go unseen. Zacxh wondered if that might be some latent ancestral ability which Sorn would one day discover.

The voyage to Karsolithuyl went quickly and without incident. The Spiderguard was met with only minimal resistance at the gate, though the outpost was well designed to repel attack. The guards demanded an explanation as to the Spiderguard’s purpose but Inarra used her considerable charms to seduce and beguile the pliant males into allowing entry. She promised them 'attention' after her bath. They provided enthusiastic escort.

The Karsolithuyl bathhouse put Nerr’tenden’s to shame. The water was fresher, better regulated for temperature and had not even a trace of the sulphuric smell which tainted the water in Nerr’tenden. The attendants were more civil and better skilled in the art and courtesies of the bath, and the chilled wine they brought was so delicious that even Zacxh did not abstain. This was an activity which nourished the spirit, and Zacxh emerged himself fully...

After the Spiderguard had settled into baths (Sorn took care but failed to be discreet about ogling Inarra as she disrobed for her soak), an authoritative female came to call. She defied good manners and what was in most places considered strict protocol by barging in fully armed and armored. She introduced herself as Ttt, the Captain of the Karsolithuyl guard and dismissed Zacxh with a typically female arrogance when he bluntly pointed out that she was really being quite rude and should disrobe and join them in the waters if she intended to visit. The combination of hot water, cool wine, and another supremely manipulative and condescending female put Zacxh into a fairly dangerous mood. He had an idea that this visit to Karsolithuyl was doomed to a violent conclusion and as he rested in the bath surrounded by his friends Zacxh felt the battle might as well begin sooner rather than later. The fact that he was naked and unarmed made little difference. He was in no mood to be patronized or even disturbed by this rude intruder.

Inarra gave away little of the circumstances surrounding the Spiderguard’s unannounced arrival in Karsolithuyl. She implied that they came on vague house business to pass through the area and that she and her friends only stopped due to the presence of Illithid in the area. She also made a point to mention that she and her companions had saved the lives and cargo of Karsolithuyl latest caravan which was led by Uuu. Inarra explained that he had promised save harbor by way of thanks.

At this Ttt became exceedingly cordial. She asked about the wellbeing of Uuu with whom she was obviously having an affair, and thanked the Spiderguard extravagantly (for a female) for his safe deliverance from the Mind Flayers.

The attitude of the meeting chanced in light of the caravan rescue and Ttt invited the Guard to stay as her guests. More specifically, she invited Sorn Nal and Valron (by far the most beautiful males of the guard) to join her 'anytime' for a 'private meeting.' No sooner had she finished speaking but Sorn leapt to his feet and indicated he was ready to depart for a 'meeting.' Naked and bathed in the harsh candlelight of the baths, it was obvious that he was indeed ready. Embarrassingly so.

The pair departed for many hours during which Inarra became more and more agitated. Apparently Sorns claims of bedding the gorgeous scout were more than mere boasts.

The following day, as Zacxh and the rest again basked in the opulent luxury of the Karsolithuyl baths, Ttt returned and assigned a guard to escort them to wherever they would care to tour. Apparently Sorn had made a very favorable impression. He was apparently quite skilled in *all* the forms of dance and Ttt made it clear that she looked forward to his extended stay.

Setting aside all the hanky panky and thoughts of rampant homicide, the actual reason for the Spiderguard's visit was to investigate the mystery of the tattoos found on insurgents in both Ossund and Orlylyl. The words on the tattoo matched too closely with the Karsolithuyl house motto to be coincidence. To that end Valron plied the bath attendants for information about tattoos and such, but he was either too obtuse, or the attendants were too astute or discreet. Valron learned nothing.

The guard which Ttt assigned, on the other hand, turned out to be a windfall of sorts. As Inarra plied him with her charms, Zacxh caught a glimpse of a tattoo which seemed to match those of the spies. A fiasco soon followed.

Inarra and Zacxh jumped into their distracting and infuriating routine. Zacxh informed the guide that he was rude to join them in a bathing chamber clothed and armed, while Inarra did a passable job trying to seduce him out of his clothes. She was pawing and rubbing him all over trying to better expose his incriminating tattoo when Ttt burst into the chamber. She was furious about something and began tossing around accusations of spying and taking advantage of her hospitality. She was entirely correct of course still, the change in her demeanor was pretty shocking. Especially so, thought Zacxh, because it occurred during a relaxing soak in the baths. He wondered how she could risen to the post of Captain and yet have so little regard for decorum.

Zacxh grudgingly hauled himself from his interrupted soak and began dressing. Inarra continued to verbally fence with the steward looking for some opportunity to learn more of the spies, or to at least cause more trouble. She scored another direct hit when she mentioned that she would enjoy meeting the steward to thank him or her personally for the hospitality. Ttt of course could not deny the request, but muttered something foreboding about such a meeting not to be attempted by the sane.

Spiderguard was led to the steward's chambers under heavy guard. She was not at all what Zacxh expected. Her demeanor was grandmotherly and her attitude distracted and impatient in a strange mixture which left one thinking that she was either completely inept or insane with underutilized power. Zacxh Liked her, thought on the Inept or insane issue, he assumed the latter.

She invited Spiderguard into her generous quarters, apparently afflicted with the addiction of all stewards... Tea. She passed around little cakes on a small platter and clapped her hands to begin the arduous ceremony.

The Spiderguard settled in and made small talk with the ancient elf. She was impatient to have them all settled and issued terse, grandmotherly commands.

Once everyone was settled and behaving like nice little murderers, the tea began. All sense of urgency dissipated as the very formal ritual began. Two stooped servants appeared from behind beautiful marble columns with servings concocted from a subtle blend if herbs and fungus. Zacxh looked to Sorn and Valron who seemed pleased with the aromatic stuff. They sipped in respectful silence of the ritual. Zacxh looked into the murky water in his cup and sniffed. He was not impressed and set the tea down untried. He appreciated the ceremony much more than the actual beverage and now that the formalized stooping and bowing was complete, had no real need for or interest in the few sips before him.

The steward began making small talk.

'It is interesting that the bag did not mention your coming. Usually it foretells of all visitors.'

This was the second reference to the mysterious 'bag.' This time there was no escaping the discussion. Inarra was clearly intrigued and seized the opportunity to find out more about this strange thing.

'Yes... Hmm... That does seem strange' She began. 'Well maybe 'the bag' did not know we were coming...

'Impossible, the bag sees and knows all.' The steward was incredulous at the suggestion.

Inarra, as always, stirred the pot a bit. 'Perhaps we could meet the bag and ask it.'

The steward froze in contemplation. She sat statue still a moment and the shrugged in resignation. 'Yes perhaps that is a good idea...'

Zacxh knew nothing of 'the bag' but was sure that 'meeting' it was probably going to be a bad idea.

The steward clapped her hands again and after only the briefest moment, a stooped servant appeared with a large silken pillow upon which lay a medium sized nondescript leather bag. The Spiderguard watched in rapt silence as the steward placed the bag into the center of her chamber and with her mouth hovering over the opening whispered a few phrases. She stepped back a pace or so and waited. The bag erupted.

The figure which emerged did so violently. If a genie pops out of a bottle in a cloud of smoke and a summoned hell hound steps from its native plane through a glowing portal then this thing arrived from the bag from whatever burning pit of hell it called home much as an elephant would emerge from the anus of a hummingbird. The arrival of the bag's inhabitant was one of the most unlikely and disturbing sights Zacxh could remember.

Ten feet of heavily muscled torso thrust forth stretching the now mucousy looking and elastic mouth of the bag well past its probable limits. It looked like a potato grub birthing an armless pig. The torso was topped by a bald head with cruel glowing eyes. The demons arms were grotesquely thin and under formed and tipped with fetid nails on long boney fingers. The demon’s mouth twisted into an annoyed scowl and the words which burst out in a powerful baritone shook the walls like an earthquake.

'WHY HAVE YOU AGAIN DISTURBED A B C D E F G!!!'

'That,' explained The steward in an almost bored tone 'is the Bag.'

The Spiderguard were all instantly on their feet reflexively stepping back a bit. This was definitely not what anyone had expected. Zacxh stood still as a stone and watched the demon with a professional eye. He wondered if the thing could be hurt and if he would be forced to find out. It was clearly a denizen of a darker and more sinister world and its presence here in Karsolithuyl seemed wrong on many levels.

Zacxh looked about to see the reaction of his companions. most had a shocked look to them and just starred, but Sorn was severely agitated, and looked like he was trying to disappear behind Trynn. Zacxh's suspicions were confirmed. The dancer definitely faded from view a bit and Zacxh caught a glimpse of stone wall right thought the little elf.

The demon glowered at the steward, then seemed to bristle a bit as if it had just heard an intriguing sound or noticed something familiar. It looked away from the steward and spun upon Sorn. It gazed directly at Sorn almost as if Trynn were not interposing the view at all.

It almost seemed to smile as it spoke.

'VENGANCE LITTLE ONE... YOU ONLY NEED ASK AND VENGANCE SHALL BE YOURS!'

Sorn cowered behind Trynn, but could not escape as the demon reached out its tiny arm. The arm was far to short to reach but the entire dimension of the room warped and constricted. The arm did not seem to stretch so much as the distance between the Demon and Sorn seemed to shrink. It touched Sorn’s shoulder and the two of them flowed like a pink, meaty vortex back into the tortured little bag. The Spiderguard was left gawking.

The steward was first to speak.

'Hmm. It has never done *that* before... Well, I guess that concludes tea, perhaps you all had better be on your way.'

Zacxh spoke up quickly. He hoped to set the tone for the verbal barrage which was sure to come from Inarra.

'Yes, well tea was lovely ma'am indeed, but perhaps we might impose upon your hospitality a bit longer to try and recover the elf your bag just... um... ate. He is after all an important member of our expedition.'

As expected, Inarra chimed in.

'Oh yes, our good friend Sorn cannot be left to this fate...'

Innara began her typical tactic of speaking of everything and nothing all the while watching the stewards face for some reaction to exploit. The Stewart seemed totally disinterested in Sorn's well being and was merely interested in the Bag's unusual behavior. Nonetheless Inarra convinced her to let the Spiderguard remain in her quarters while she tried a few things to sort the matter out.

The Stewart put her face back into the bag and began muttering for the demons return. She stayed at it much longer this time, and just when Zacxh was beginning to wonder if the Demon had somehow escaped its prison, the bag erupted again. This time it sent the steward sprawling back. Sorn stood at the 'feet' of the demon and looked a bit like he was enjoying himself. The demon spoke again.

'I SHALL DESTROY THE DESTROYERS. I SHALL AVENGE YOUR LOSS. JUST SAY THE WORD AND THE RECKONING SHALL BEGIN.'

Sorn looked as if he had consumed too much tea. His face was bright, his back straight. and his eyes seemed to have taken on a glow of their own much like those of the demon which hovered over the dancer like a protective parent. No one knew what to do and no one moved. Sorn looked apologetically toward Valron and uttered the command which he knew would spell doom.

'Valron, the Illithid amass outside the gates, we must be careful... '

He paused and looked about the room.

'Yes ABCDEFG, give me vengeance!'

The room went inky black with vile demonic energy. Somewhere a strange voice called out and the steward's guards began to die. Zacxh closed his eyes and reached out with his mind's eye to feel for the life force of those around him. He was suddenly acutely aware of all the hate and pain and fear around him. The room and every inhabitant therein appeared to his mind outlined by the ghosts of their repressed and most horrible memories. Zacxh drew his blade and cut off a guard who was groping forward trying to reach the steward. Zacxh felt his scars bristle and his arms swell with power as he hacked the guard down in the darkness.

The captain of the guard burst into the darkened room from her post just outside and was immediately attacked by the demon. The steward chanted some sort of spell and the Spiderguard for the most part drew back to the walls unsure of which threat to attack.

Zacxh ran past the Captain expertly slashing her from shoulder to shoulder. His blade cleaved through her armor but even blinded by the demon’s oppressive darkness, she twisted out of the way of most of the damage. She was a very skilled warrior, and got off with a fairly superficial wound. Sorn blasted the Captain with a bolt of his own dark energy which to Zacxh's mind eye appeared as a dark bolt of pure hate. The usually ineffective stuff slammed into the captain and drained much of her spiritual reserves. Sorn Grinned Evilly.

The Steward completed her incantation and the inky darkness which the demon had wrought constricted and coalesced into a dark ball in her upraised fist. She held the wad of hateful energy a moment before releasing it into a ray which slammed the demon mightily.

The demon roared in anger and reached out his tiny arm in that unsettling, space warping way, and slashed the steward across the chest with glowing claws. Where the nails found flesh, lines of blue demonic flame remained to burn on painfully. The steward seemed only vaguely aware of the attack and commented in an intrigued voice.

'Hmm it has never done that before either... how odd'

Zacxh attacked a nearby guard. He caught it off guard in all the confusion and nearly bisected the elf from neck to hip. Combat was joined all around between the Spiderguard, Sorn’s demon, and the steward with her guards. Zacxh charged the steward but was stopped in his tracks by the demon. The infernal beast's claws raked across Zacxh's chest, tore through the iron hardness of his scars as if they were not even there, and left three burning lines scraped into his skin. Pain and light erupted from the wound and Zacxh found himself wounded, and engulfed in demonic flame.

He called out enraged to Sorn.

'Hey Dancer, control that thing before it kills us all.'

Zacxh was suddenly acutely aware that his life was in serious danger. If those flames continued for too long they would overwhelm his minds ability to fend them off and begin devouring his flesh. He retreated into a corner, took up a defensive stance and began rummaging around his mind for a solution to his dilemma. He poured himself inward, but left enough sense behind to ward off attack. If that demon reached out for him again, it would loose at a finger. Zacxh did not want to feel those claws again.

His back against the wall, Zacxh ran the corridors of his mind looking for a means of fending off the flames. He did not have to look far and discovered a new trick.

The answer was, as always, provided by painful memories of his past. He focused his mind on the revulsion he felt about being consumed by flame and remembered a dozen occasions when he had been disfigured by the heat of brands and coals. His fears and revulsions, so central to his psyche, did the rest. Zacxh was vaguely aware that the battle had changed tempo and opened his eyes to survey the scene. The steward was dead and the demon gone. Bodies were strewn about the chamber and only the Spiderguard remained. Sorn looked a bit sheepish.

Zacxh looked to his burning chest and watched as his unconscious mind took over the fight. His skin closed over and the flames were pushed away from his body by the pure force of his revulsion to being burned. Unfortunately, the energy of the heat still built within Zacxh's mind. He needed a way to dissipate it quickly before it attacked his soul just like the flames had attacked his flesh. He knew what would happen, and knew his friends were not going to like it.

'Spiderguard! Close your eyes!!!' Zacxh already had his squeezed tight and was still seeing the world in shades of hate and anger through his mind's eye.

Things were about to get interesting. Now that they were tamed, those demonic flames were about to become his blazing ticket out of there. He only hoped that they would last long enough to do some good. Now it was Zacxh who was grinning.

last edited 2006-08-19 14:59:57 by Cliff

ChapterFive

CHAPTER 5. DINNER

Zacxh pushed his legs to move faster toward the mines despite the ache and complaint of his bloated sloshing belly. He stopped for a moment, sighed then vomited violently. Beautifully prepared fish ejected with great velocity riding on a warm current of delicately spiced mushroom soup of the finest quality. Zacxh spit once to clear his palate.

'Damn shame. That was good soup.'

He pressed into a short sprint to catch his trotting companions. Running was much more comfortable now. He felt foolish to have thought the captain had invited the Spiderguard for an actual dinner, and now having thought about it, it was almost predictable that his beautiful meal was laying in a ditch and he was chasing down another vile enemy of the house.

That was okay with Zacxh. The dinner show had been a bit tedious anyhow. He would rather stretch his legs in pursuit of sport than watch a royal daughter of house Oussund whip her servants to death. The novelty of that sort of show had worn off for Zacxh decades ago.

Trynn had looked so very concerned. It was as if he thought Zacxh might sep up to intervene. Trynn was naive in the way's of Lolth’s chosen. He thought the Priestess might have some feeling about the beating that she was taking some pleasure in it. Zacxh knew better. He knew that the priestess took no more pleasure and gave no more thought to the needless death that Zacxh gave to tying a shoe. It was just a tedious necessary chore. Even the show of fury as she hurled the bludgeoned body off the balcony. Nothing but a show. Like one of Inarra’s fits of sexual ecstasy... just a show.

Zacxh moved his thoughts to the task at hand. His quarry.

...Zacxh crept down the hallway. The weak, and feinting stone shaper who had run from dinner turned out to be some sort of insurgent. He had broken into Captain Xulleyl's quarters to destroy some evidence, and was now holding out deep in the mines.

Already Sorn and Inarra were looking defeated. They motioned to Zacxh the stone shaper mage was further down the passage, and cautioned that it was wielding nasty flying disks. They were nursing some pretty serious looking wounds.

Zacxh pulled up his concealing cloak and crept further along. Valron was right on his heels. It was comforting to have him near.

Zacxh had to smile about the so called 'discipline' of his crew. They had spent the last few weeks drilling on how to take certain formations and assume certain predictable roles in combat. Above all they had resolved to move and to try to act and think as one. In the arena that had all begun to work. In the arena.

Tonight, the Spidergaurd had been 'invited to dinner.' Nominally, they were there to celebrate the cleansing of the mines and to be recognized both by the Steward of Nerr’tenden and by the Stone shapers whose powerful rods had been recovered with the rest of the loot.

When Captain Xulleyl had first extended the 'invitation,' It seemed plausible, if only barely so. Now Zacxh new better. The dinner conversation about the head table, which of course seated all the dignitaries well away from the Spidergaurd, flirted around deceptions about what was recovered and when the rods were to be handed over. In retrospect it was clear that Captain Xulleyl expected some sort of trouble and had the Spiderguard on hand to head it off. Perhaps she had overestimated their abilities.

The Spiderguard all knew their roles and formations and Zacxh was their 'tactical commander.' Then one of the dignitaries departed early and after another course of soup and wine, Inarra started whispering to Sorn. Before Zacxh knew what was happening, half the guard was running for the door and the other half were trying to covertly gain the attention of the captain. Once all was said and done, guard members were spread all over Nerr’tenden and beyond, toward the mines, Captain Xulleyl looked mildly bemused and annoyed and Zacxh knowing little of what was transpiring, only that there was a Xulleyl imposter running around town, was patiently slurping his soup. Ah the soup. Such a waste.

So there he was, creeping up upon what was presumably a powerful and battle ready mage. Zacxh paused a moment and dove deep into the safe recesses of his mind. He awakened old pain and fear to run rampant in the untended parts of his mind. He waited while those old daemons gave strength and resolve to his flesh. after a moment he felt calm and dispassionate but wore an enraged body ready for war. It was a good thing too, for just as he crept around the next corner leading to the old insurgents headquarters, a shuriken slammed into his shoulder with enough force to nearly spin him around. It was like being hit by a club. The wind was knocked out of Zacxh but his infuriated flesh pressed on.

'Look out! Shuriken!' he gasped out while gulping for air.

Zacxh sprinted for cover ahead around the next corner. He pressed against the rocks and used his cloak to melt into the stone. He did not relish the thought of being hammered by more of those amazing missiles.

Across the room, Zacxh could see other guard members moving up to join him in cover. He watched them, feeling secure in his cover when four more shuriken came hurtling toward him. Two hit the rocks, behind which he crouched, but two hit him with the force of hammers. He saw stars and slumped to the floor. His last thought before several moments of senselessness was that the damn disk launching mage was either invisible or able to hurl disks around the corner. Either way, despite armor, thickened skin and mental barriers, the disks had hit him with enough force that they would have killed most members of the guard. Zacxh was much tougher than most, but still the force of the attack was staggering.

This was not going to be a fair fight. Unlike his battles in the pits, Zacxh realized he had the opportunity to withdraw if need be. He did not like that idea. First he would test the water with this 'mage.'

Zacxh refocused his mind. He felt his hurts fall away and the fury within his mind force his bruised body to alertness. He would act as a barrier for his guard, drawing the fire of this frightening foe so that his team could try to find some weakness or advantage. It was not going to be pleasant. Zacxh focused on the image of the bear which was so powerfully in his dreams of late. He specifically focused his mind on that aspect of the bear which made it so resilient, its bulk and stability and sheer force of spirit.

He waited a moment. Then his body began to respond. His loose cut garments began to squeeze and stretch with his increased bulk. His huge sword felt like a toy in his bulging and furry hands.

Normally, he would well overmatch a foe in this state. This time... well, unless Nal or some other spell caster could find a chink in this guy's defense, retreat was fast becoming the option.

Zacxh hoped that perhaps their might be some way to let the mage go and tail him to find out what he was up to here in the mines. He wondered if maybe it was time to let the scouts earn their pay.

last edited 2006-02-26 01:19:41 by Eric

ChapterFour

CHAPTER 4. AFTERMATH

Emails

Inarra leaned heavily against the wall after her mental assault on the enemy captain, skin flushed and one cheek smudged prettily. She watched his face contort, and then he fell as if in slow motion, Xulleyl stepping back out of his way. Inarra's eyes snapped to the seriously injured Xulleyl, who moved to the nearest wall. Xulleyl's skin and equipment were smoldering and cracked from the fireball's detonations, her lungs heaved wetly with the ragged holes the sword had made on its passage through her body. Two more cuts bled heavily from her side and weapon arm.

Xulleyl let the wall hold up her weight while she retrieved a small leathery packet from a tiny belt pouch. She opened the top and poured a fine powder into her mouth, then swallowed. Her wounds didn't appear any better, but she seemed to gain some strength from the dose. She carefully closed the packet and replaced it in the tiny belt pouch. She moved back to the fallen enemy and cleaned her blade on his cloak, then sheathed it in a single fluid motion.

Standing erect, she quickly walked back down the passage, snapping an order back over her shoulder: "Bring him." She walked on without looking back.

Zacxh had the dead captain draped over his shoulder as he walked down the hallway. He was visibly injured though his face betrayed no trace of pain, as always it was expressionless and bland.

His leg was torn open by a wicked sword slash, and he bled from three or four other nasty cuts. Three crossbow bolts protruded from various locations; one snapped off at the shaft, presumably to allow him the movement of his right arm. His new fine cloths were torn in several locations by sword cuts that did not seem to leave any mark on the underlying flesh and every scar on his body stood up angrily. He trailed an odor of ozone and burnt hair and small wisps of smoke traced the passage of both he and his charred cargo as he limped down the corridor.

The Spidergaurd rallied about their severely injured Captain and in the several inevitable moments of rushed orders and consolidation, Zacxh found himself standing near Kadyel.

He looked at her as if to speak actually quirking his eyebrow a moment, then decided better. Without comment he hefted the dead captain onto his smoldering shoulder and moved off toward the 'Headquarters'. The dripping trail of blood he left behind would not be difficult to follow.

Clearly burned and torn up, but nonetheless the proud glint remaining in her eye, Kadyel smiles at Zacxh as she catches up to him. "We fought well today," she says quietly to him, noticing his reticence. "I know you have no trust for me. However, I think we of the Spiderguard have more reason to trust each other than any of our masters." She glances askance toward the Captain, who leads the party up ahead. "Know that I think you fought with honor. And your attention to my wounds last night was noted. Consider this my olive branch." Kadyel pats Zacxh on the back in camaraderie, expending her last spell of the day and healing him 6 points of damage. Once the dark shadow of the healing magic fades into Zacxh's wounds, she moves to grabs the dead captain's legs and together carry the body.

Zacxh closes his eyes and exhales slowly as the curative magic works through him.

'Six more like that and we will be even...'

He watches as the fury just begins to build in Kadyel then quickly smiles.

'Easy there! I am kidding.'

Thanks for the healing. It is much needed. I have not felt this beaten in a long while.'

'I agree that we showed well today. And thank you for your kind words. I gave all I had today. I was not sure it would be enough.'

'Would you welcome a friendly word of caution? I believe you acted in good faith with your powerful magics today and truly do not begrudge your judgment error in blowing me halfway to hell. After all it was a desperate struggle.'

'I am not sure our captain sees it that way. I alone was in a position to see her face after taking the full brunt of your fireball. It looked to me like she was momentarily torn between killing her foe and coming back to dispatch her wayward mage...'

'You might think about watching your manners with her awhile. I don't need tell you that she can be pretty damn dangerous... And she knows where you live.'

'Perhaps you are right about me. Perhaps I am too trusting. It may well be my undoing, but let me also propose that your lack of confidence in any but yourself may very well be yours.'

'I am unfamiliar with your reference to an 'olive branch'... Sounds like a reference to burn elves... But if you imply that we might set aside the fact that we got off on the wrong foot... Well I am happy to agree.'

'I feel compelled to apologize again for insulting you. That whole 'viper pit of lies and deceit' thing was poorly spoken. Truly I meant it as a complement to your ability to think around problems that my warrior’s instinct would have me attack front on.'

'I tire of all this arguing and misunderstanding, so let me just say this in parting. Even though you may pledge nothing to the Spidergaurd. I will extend my meager protection to you. I hope you will soon return the favor.'

'For now, let me carry this piece of meat. I don't want to be in the blast area if the captain decides she has been too charitable with you.'

Zacxh gives Kadyel a wink and strides off with the large dead captain slung easily over his shoulder.

Zacxh has a quiet word in the corner with Inarra then walks boldly to the common area table and leaps lightly upon it. Despite his many and obvious wounds and the fact that he looks like he has fallen face down into a raging bonfire he is light on his feet and amazingly full of life. In fact he appears as a well rested elf wearing merely the costume of a battered, burnt and bleeding train wreck victim.

'Okay Spidergaurd, we are all desperately in need a trip to the bathhouse which I am happy to say can be easily and well arranged by Valron. (A bow to Valron) But first things first. As your designated liaison to the Captain I propose we quickly dispense with petty, greedy concerns and merely do as she has asked. I have thought of many solutions to how we should divvy up and retain all this loot, and am at a loss to know which is best. So. I propose the following. We dump it all on this here table. Get it all identified. Tithe whatever the captain deems as her own then allocate the rest to whoever can best use it. For example. Armor and swords to the brawlers. Sneaky boots and daggers to the scouts, magic hats and... Wands... (an uncharacteristic wink to Kadyel) to the mages etc. etc.

Anything we do not need, I propose be liquidated and put into a 'Company fund' to pay for arms, armor, healing, feasts, the bathhouse and so on.'

'I can see from some of your reactions that letting the Captain have first pick of the loot is rubbing some of you the wrong way. I will absolutely not insist on any of this. It is merely a proposal. However, if you will indulge me, I will make my case.'

'I hope to glean from this first gesture of subservience whether or not the Captain values our contribution to the fight or weather we are but disposable tools. If she lets us keep our salvaged equipment and so arm ourselves, we will know something of our worth to her. If not...'

'My second point is that without the Captain, I for one, and by my estimation the bulk of the rest of you would be rat meat right about now. If she takes it all, my sensibilities would not be overwrought.'

'Finally, our esteemed Captain is a scout. I doubt there is much that could go unaccounted for that she would not miss. I tried that once already to poor effect.'

'These are my points. I am in no position to insist upon them, but I will say this...'

'Perhaps my faith in the Captain is misplaced. I do not think so, but perhaps. At any rate, I will place my only real treasure as collateral on this faith.'

'If the Captain sees fit to unfairly pillage our hard won plunder, I will barter my stealth cloak to the merchants of Nerr’tenden and throw the proceeds into our company fund as a gesture of goodwill, and afterward will gladly indulge in any subterfuge you see fit to retain our wealth.'

'So, what do you think?'

Zacxh dumps a large sack full of loot that no one but Valron has yet seen on the table. Mixed into the generous pile of platinum and gold (hundreds) are rings, amulets, Fine looking boots, another cloak, necklaces and a generous pile of gems a masterwork dagger and whatnot.

'Don't be shy now; you might even come out ahead in this deal...'

He arranges the piles of coin into neat stacks and arranges the other treasure into easily recognizable groups and piles.

Sorn quickly sorts the valuables and equipment into piles. His eyes widen at the items contributed from Zacxh's bag, putting many of them into the magical pile. There are also two locked boxes, one similar to the already-opened box of coins (and it sounds like it's full of coins as well); the other is of the same size and make as the poison case. Sorn and Len we are able to spend a few minutes and open them; the coin box is definitely difficult to get but Sorn has already opened its twin and it soon surrenders to his gentle ministrations...

The resulting hoard is intimidating to even the most jaded among you; you have clearly taken the resources of a well-stocked force.

Money, Gems and Jewelry 198 platinum 597 gold 1,210 silver 1,650 copper 2 pouches full of small common gems 2 bracelets 3 rings 2 pairs of earrings 2 necklaces

Special Equipment masterwork chain shirt matched pair of throwing daggers masterwork hand crossbow an unlocked small box with a DC 25 lock, no key two cases of poisons

Magical Items masterwork short sword necklace of copper and gold 2 fine cases, 2 ft long, 3 inches by 3 inches clasped with enruned silverwork worked silver ring 3 vials with liquid in them masterwork dagger boots of very fine make bracers of battered silver beautiful embroidered cape fine powder in a folded piece of paper sapphire pendant leather bracelet with jade inlay

Trynn is remarkably more composed now that we have returned to the barracks. No more twitchy glances or strange mutterings or staring suspiciously at blank walls. His voice is steadier and he appears generally more in control.

Trynn sheepishly pulls an unremarkable hand crossbow from his belt and lays it on the table. It is fairly worn and of average quality. He speaks while looking down at the floor, too ashamed to make eye contact with Zacxh standing up there on the table who is eyeing Trynn with amusement no doubt.

"I apologize Spiderguard. I took this from Burl for myself. I've never owned anything so fine and ... well. .. I thought no one would mind but there it is. I was wrong to try to take such valuable plunder for my own."

He glances up briefly at Kadyel before mustering the courage to look Zacxh in the eye. "My selfish lapse of discipline will not happen again, Spiderguard. Do not let this taint your opinion of me. I swear by Lolth's bloated belly, you can all rely on me."

Zacxh's face if it could hold any expression at all would indeed hold amusement. Instead, his look is its usual bland stare.

Zacxh toes the crossbow into the pile of loot.

'Not to worry Trynn, there was no prohibition on using dropped weapons. I am only recommending that we account for them. I think it is safe to say you should take it as your own once we have all this stuff tallied.

Zacxh drops lightly from the table, and with a friendly hand on Trynn's shoulder works to sort the loot as it is dumped on the table. After a minute or two, his unbelievable stamina fades leaving him looking worn and battle weary.

Absentmindedly fingering the dead soldier's necklace that he now wears, Sorn looks at Kadyel, a mixture of fear and defiance in his expression.

"It's not like it was a wand of brimstone, Trynn."

He holds Kadyel's unflinching gaze for a moment longer, then lowers his eyes.

"I am exhausted, and I will think better on all of this after a soak in the baths and some sleep on something more comfortable than hard ground. Can the inventory wait until tomorrow?"

I appreciate your sentiment Sorn, and it is up to you of course, but I for one would prefer to take my soak with an easy mind having dispensed with our commitment to the Captain. She asked that we array our haul and call for her as soon as we are ready to debrief. I will rest easier with those chores completed, and suspect that your new jewelry as well as your presence will make that imminent encounter go more smoothly.

There is much to be done before I retire for the day. I need to deliver this (a gesture to the smoldering body), and hope to compile and deliver a report of any noteworthy observations about the happenings in the mines. Having observed and having performed some horrible swordsmanship today, I think I'd better request more training for us as well.

I have crossed paths with Lt. Ardul several times this week. He is a petty and vindictive little shit and I don't think he will be acting as a swordsmanship instructor for us any longer... At least not in the training ring. (a small smile flits across Zacxh’s blank face)

At any rate, let's get through this nonsense so we can enjoy our evening. Perhaps while we rest I can arrange to have any magical properties riddled out of this shining heap of plunder. Once that is done you may find one of the other baubles more to your liking. (a gesture to a small handful of rings and amulets which came from Zacxh's sack.)

Speaking of which, unless there are any objections, I will use some of the coins here to pay for any magicians fees. Inarra, perhaps you are better suited than I to negotiating the price.

Zacxh looks Sorn in the eye only for a moment inviting his reply... And his jewelry.

Sorn doesn't have any trouble meeting and holding the heavily scarred warrior's gaze, though he can't completely mask his fear.

"Tss! Very well, Zacxh. I will agree to separate the riches from the rubbish before we take our much deserved baths. Though, quite frankly, you look to be more in need of one than most."

Sorn moves the coin and jewels aside and begins, flippantly, to sort the company's loot into three groups. Into one, he carelessly heaps a large number of unremarkable items. He places a number of items of obvious quality and craftsmanship, including most of the masterwork arms and armor, into another pile. Sorn then places a mixture of items--including a beautifully made short sword that belonged to Burl's sergeant--into a third group, and these he lays out carefully, side-by-side.

When he finishes separating the valuables, Sorn looks steadily at Zacxh, a mixture of anger, fear and grudging respect on his face. He reaches around and unclasps the claimed necklace with, then places it gently with the third group of treasure.

"These are enchanted," he states plainly, waving with a long-fingered hand to indicate the carefully laid out items. "The others are not. Now that we have determined what makes sense to further inspect, I will gladly negotiate my fee with Inarra...a task for which she is indeed *far* better suited.

Zacxh holds Sorn’s gaze a moment taking in the anger and fear.

"Please don't look at me like that sir. I am merely trying to comply with the desires of our Captain. As we all know, our lives are in her hands, and I think the more compliant and effective we are, the better our chances to win privilege."

Zacxh glances to the unlocked door.

"So, I, as your servant and messenger will now take our report and go. I will also take that burnt body and my own to tell our deadly captain that we have sorted the loot and that we are ready for inspection... With your permission."

"Good luck with your negotiation. I suspect your biggest battle of the day is yet to come..."

"Oh, and about the bath..." Zacxh looks at his blood crusted and smelling arms. "I could not agree more."

Zacxh takes one more appraising look at the table, heaves the dead elven barbeque upon his shoulder and with a hopeful glance at Valron to follow, moves to depart.

Having remained silent throughout the discussion of spoils, Nal steps forward as Zacxh tries to leave.

"Perhaps it would be best if a representative of each expedition to Nerr'tenden accompanied you to provide a complete report as the Captain requested. I would welcome the opportunity to exercise our newfound liberty myself, in any case."

"Absolutely."

Zacxh scarcely slows his stride until reaching the door then holds it deferentially for Nal.

Kadyel speaks on their departure, "Nal, please make sure to be as complete as possible. I'm sure Xulleyl will appreciate any detail I left out when I debriefed her as you were interrogating our last prisoner. You may let her know I am at her disposal should she want any more info from me." She smiles wanly.

Sorn speaks again.

"Inarra and Kadyel, do you both wish that I represent our group's journey to Nerr'tenden and accompany Nal and Zacxh?"

Zacxh's lifeless eyes suddenly awaken. He raises his gaze from its respectful down turned angle to glare at Sorn.

'You are becoming a real pain in my ass elf.'

Zacxh hefts the mangled Captain's corpse to the floor with enough force that it let's out a dead man’s moan.

'Here. Take this pile of gore and take your suspicions, and take your goddamned necklace as well. Relay our shared knowledge, which amounts about to SQUAT! and go see the Captain. Oh, while you are at it, don't forget to give her Kadyel's sniveling regards. And on your way you can take my thanks as well. That body reeks and is giving me a crick in to neck. I hope you enjoy hauling it. Her door is the last on the right. Knock and wait to be summoned.'

Zacxh glares at all of you.

'I have tried to serve and protect you. I had hoped that by doing so I might earn your trust and your eventual protection so I could sleep without fear of having my neck parted. We'll you sniveling bickering heap of pansy assed bootlickers are beyond hope. Trying to guide you into a position of influence in this piss ant town is like trying to herd cats. I have done nothing but be loyal to you and serve you. Well now I have had it. I merely go to FETCH our damned Captain and am to be followed by an entourage of paranoid overseers. Screw it. Fetch her yourself. I'm sure she is in as good a mood as I after being blown nearly in half by her own Spidergaurd.'

Zacxh strolls to a corner and pulls out his boot knife. He uses it to scrape the blood out from under his grubby fingernails. When he notices anyone watching, he nods encouragingly to the door.

'Go on you distrusting bastards. Run your own errands. See how well the reaper responds to your bowing and scraping, but don't ever say I didn't warn you.'

Zacxh's face deadens and his angered breathing stills. He is dispassionate as he pulls, at long last, the one remaining crossbow bolt he has been sporting from out of his calf. He doesn't even wince.

Kadyel speaks quietly to Zacxh in the hallway, on her way to her room for weapon cleanup. "Your talent for theatrics is noted, friend. Know that it is not my mistrust of you that forced my speech earlier. Nal is the least spoken and most unnerving of all of us. And his choices in our encounters before your arrival were not wise. It is him I trust least at this point."

Sorn glances over his shoulder to take in the expressions on the others' faces, wondering for a moment if maybe he's the crazy one. Then he sighs heavily and struggles to get the lifeless body of the enemy captain up over his shoulder. The young elf almost goes down, but then manages to get the extra weight balanced over his dancer's legs. He moves towards the open door, not bothering to look at Zacxh as he passes by.

As Sorn passes through the doorway, he remarks, "Half of the stuff on this body is enchanted. If the captain gives the okay, I will return with all of it."

Listening to see if Nal is following, Sorn moves to shuffle down the hall with obvious difficulty.

Zacxh looks up absently from binding his leg and calls after Sorn.

'I am a killer, I am a pit fighter, and until recently I was a slave.'

'I am not a diplomat, nor do I indulge in the mincing of words. I will tell you straight what I think and would rather cut you down where you stand than expend the effort to try and puff up the air with lies and intrigue'

'I really don't give a burners crap who walks down the hall with that body to summon our captain. If you want to go, than go. Her instructions were to arrange the haul, deliver the body, figure out what clues we might have to illuminate the situation in the mine, and to summon her.'

'Unless you think I am going to add to the phrase 'here is the body sir, and we are ready' some sort of insidious poisonous intrigue, then why do you care who comes along. I asked Valron to attend me only as protection from Lt. Ardul who is out for my blood.'

'Now, if you want me to pick that bleeding rag up for you and lead some paranoid parade to our Captains quarters, you need merely ask. But remember this. I serve you all as to make the Spidergaurd stronger. Nothing more. If you don't trust me even to act as delivery boy then make your own deliveries. Arrange your own training. By all means hoard and covet and steal all the loot you want. We will all die paranoid and alone. You will find a knife to your throat before you see your next year.'

'There are plenty of people to slake your lust for blood and lies *outside* these doors.'

'Turn that lust within, and we all die. Forgotten by history as a failed experiment.'

'Just make it quick dancer, for as you so kindly pointed out. I need a bath.'

Zacxh returns to tending his wound.

Nal gives Zacxh a pregnant look before moving to leave again. At the door, he stops to speak.

"It seems our full report will have to wait, as Sorn and I clearly cannot present every angle. Nevertheless, it seems we have produced some compelling information.

================================================ Zacxh moves to better sort the loot and mutters a few words as he works. His voice is low and weary but gains passion as he says the following to Trynn.

'Remember brother, we are slaves no longer. You can keep whatever you like from these peon insurgents. I am glad to make a full accounting of our haul, but never expect another apology from you, just as you shall never have mine. We have paid for a lifetime of unperformed transgressions, and owe the world no more. You will always have the benefit of the doubt from me.'

'It is time we cast aside our bondage and embrace the opportunity to finally live... And live well.'

'Do you want a command from me your friend and servant? Well here it is. Eat. Soak, and, *please*, sleep in a good bed tonight. You have earned it. These are the spoils of war, and just as I plan to bathe in the blood of my enemies, I plan to bath in their plunder as well. Join me. We will rock the Underdark to its foundations as we reclaim what has been taken from us!'

  • Trynn is somewhat taken aback by the forcefulness of Zacxh’s soliloquy. It is as if he has never encountered such thoughts, thoughts of living well, thoughts of taking back what has been taken from him. It's as if his whole life it never occurred to him that things could be otherwise.

    He stares at Zacxh with a mixture of respect and ... envy.

"If only I had nothing to lose, Zacxh", he whispers quietly and steps forward to help Zacxh with the chore of organizing the goods.

As they work, Trynn speaks. "Can you tell me more about this man you met from House Oussund, the one who met with Xulleyl and appeared to know all about us? Is he still here in Nerr’tenden?
