"Let me emphasize that I am no leader. I would be happy enough to steer the course of my *own* destiny. Rather I believe our survival now hinges on our ability to work together..."

"As for the `contest', I think we all learned a lot out there, especially that this is no group to be trifled with. I attribute my victory more to fate than to martial skill, and I have no great faith in the benevolence of my fate." Zacxh pauses a moment to scratch the torn and tattered remains of his right ear.

"The captain asked what we learned out there. Here is what I saw. Divided, strong though we may be, we are already defeated. So. Here is my second proposal. I propose a creed of warriors. I propose that we commit to one another here and now. We will not survive our training if we do not pull together. Individuals have no place in a group like this. I have proposed to some of you that we watch each others backs. Now I propose it to you all. Furthermore, though not a leader, I will act as watchman, and any elf who acts in a harmful way toward anyone in this room will answer to my blade."

"I expect one of two outcomes from this. Either I will be dead by the morrow, or we will become one of the great units of the Underdark. I have already been handed threats due to my unenviable position as `leader.' Well so be it. I have very little to lose in death, and if we do not pull together death is what we shall have."

Zacxh picks up the pin, stuffs it unceremoniously into his pouch and grabs a loaf of sweat bread which he stuffs into his mouth with a swig of water to chase it down.

"By the way in answer to Trynn's question, I was captured, enslaved and beaten by house Oosund. The priestesses of the house conspired and executed my demise. I hold no loyalty to anyone and claim no house. Therefore when I swear my blood to this our "Spidergaurd" there can and will be no conflict of interest."

"I believe we are all `dead'. Perhaps others of you might look at this opportunity as I have?"

Zacxh returns to his corner and resumes his servants posture. Only now, his hand rests lightly on the pommel of his well oiled and polished rapier. His eyes again appear dead.

Valron listens intently to Zacxh's speech and says to him, "Thank you for your words, they are much appreciated." He turns to address the group. "With our acquiescence to yesterday's competition, we in effect, bound ourselves to obey the rules of the Spiderguard. So I would agree that Zacxh should retain his position for this reason, regardless of how we in fact view him amongst ourselves."

Valron turns back to look Zacxh in the eye. "However, as one who was taken down swiftly by your blade, I must say that you don't give yourself enough credit, sir. In the battle we faced yesterday, you clearly proved yourself worthy in strength, bravery, and cunning. And I find the words that you have just spoken both wise and honorable. Therefore, I for one am willing to place my trust in your leadership. Far more so than I would in any...Spiderguard official I have met thus far."

Valron then eyes Trynn (eating his untreated food) with a mild disdain, "I cannot stop those of you who would prefer to place your health in the trust of Spiderguard officials rather than in the warriors of our band. However, like our leader Zacxh, I commit myself to the protection of this group. And I encourage all of you to pledge the same oath."

Zacxh eyes the floorboards with his usual deferential look and clearly blushes (an ugly medley of pink black and numerous unlikely tones of scar white)

"You are too kind and overstate the case Valron, But I appreciate your commitment to our group."

"I am not worthy to command this group. As yet I am not sure any of us are. Let me for now act as go- fer and whipping boy to the guards and warden of dangers within and without. In that capacity, I hope to help unite our band until we can find our true leader.

Inarra Choses a different morsel from the slightly dishevled array of fish.

"Hmmm, Food's not terribly bad, though the company could use some refinement[She wipes the dribble of fish juice trailed by Zacxh from the table]."

"I think this group's protestations of loyalty or not are largely irrelevant,as is the question of leadership. Clearly they would be no more than the loudest barking dog amongst a chained kennel to our 'captain', though perhaps it will be the only dog not kicked for it vocalizations [traces her bruised cheek] "

"For my part, I see no reason the elf with the largest 'stick' should not be our leader, as all we've been asked to do is whack each other. Perhaps when more subtle or thoughful decisions are called for, we can evaluate a new mouthpiece."

"And as far as group unity, I can tell I've been close with some of you already. As a matter of fact one of you saw fit to pay a midnight assignation to me. [Inarra turns and with smooth practiced ease unbuttons her shirt and lets it fall to her waist. The groups sees a fresh red slice, thin, almost surgical, stretching across her back from her right shoulder to her left hip. It is left to your imagination what a 20 Cha implies about the rest of her. She turns and slowly buttons her shirt up again].

"Now if I'd known you liked your late night assignations liked it that way, I certainly would have obliged in kind. A pity i was passed out."

"No no, protestations of innocece are not neccessary. My visitors identity was determined easily enough. There are more eyes in the dark than are known to most, and few who can talk to them."

"I'd imagine we might meet again, alone in the small hours of the dark. I do so love the feel of steel against flesh. Perhaps we shall both be awake, or perhaps not, it does make so much more exiting doesn't it?"

"Fish anyone?"

Kadyel stoped eating and regarded Zacxh for a moment before speaking.

"Loyalty and oaths are meaningless without honor and trust. Therefore I commit nothing to this group." Kadyel takes a step towards Zaxch, her steel eyes penetrating him. "It is only through action that we will begin to understand each other. And yesterday we did learn something of each other: who is best in hand-to-hand combat. But also which of us has a mind for leadership, strategy, and a will to make our own fate despite the intentions of our captors."

Kadyel turns to the others, and speaks carefully. "And it would seem that last night we learned something more, though this action upon Inarra."

She turns again to Zaxch, and speaks with sincerity, "Zaxch, I accept your offer to act as liaison. You acted yesterday with honor, and did not betray anyone. Next time you should consider the impact of your decisions on the bigger picture. But we will all learn from our time together..." she tilts her head forward in a gesture unknown to men of this world and speaks loudly for all to hear, "sir."

Leaning forward, Kadyel murmurs to the pitfighter, "Let us not overlook the fact that this wound to Inarra may be the work of our captors. For now, let us be wary, and not squeeze the juice from this mushroom before it is flowered."

In a deeply hidden and safe part of Zacxh's mind, Kadyel's bow and words strike like a thunderclap, though his absent and always detached face betray none of it. He merely continues to watch his feet as she speaks.

"Lady Kadyel, in front of all I would like to offer an apology for my words in yesterday's battle. It was well fought and I was victorious only by way of a subtle irony of fate. You are a formidable opponent. I spoke to you in a disrespectful manner during the battle. I appologize. It has been a long time since I was free of indenture and in my preocupation with newly found "freedom" I forgot myself."

Zacxh raises his blank gaze to address all. "And please Spidergaurd, do not address me as your leader. As I have said and others have agreed, I am your servant. My loyalty is to the Spidergaurd, and anyone in this room who chooses to join me in that commitment. We are not yet ready to elevate a leader, and I doubt that when the time comes if that elf will be me."

"This business with Inarra must stop. As I am not in any position to command, this is no order. It is commen sense. Without absolute faith in each other we are all doomed to lonely and certain failure."

"If Inarra choses to join in a commitment to the Spidergaurd, she will, as I have prevoiusly said, fall under its growing protection... such as it is. I loath another night slumbering with treachery."

Zacxh regards subtly powerful Inarra a moment wondering if the offer of his 'protection' is even welcome.

"Divided we are already defeated..."

Sometime after breakfast is eaten and too soon to want to move, you hear the door open and Lt. Ardul enters the room, a usual sneer on his face. “Greetings,” he says. “Suit up, let’s go.”

You are escorted out the back door by the privy (Lt. Ardul leading, the two guards following), and take the first right hand turn. The lieutenant opens the unlocked door. He leads you through a short series of turns and opens a door to a rough cavern. There is a squad of troops engaged in weapon drills when you enter. One points, and they all stop and watch you in silence as you cross the courtyard. Their faces don’t betray much, but perhaps anger, awe and jealousy flicker here and there

Ardul ignores them and leads you through a wide arch into the Nerr’tenden armory. Weapons and armor are in locked cases against the walls next to other cases full of mining tools and implements, and several apprentices are busy polishing a number of javelins. They look up with interest as you enter; Ardul takes his time, waiting for all of you to file in without speaking. A curtain opens at the far side of the armory and a tall and strong woman comes out, a tough and scarred leather apron upon her.

The lieutenant bows and says in a loud voice, “Master Shar, here are the new volunteers.” Pointing to Zacxh, he says “This one is their leader. Please outfit them.” With another bow to her, he turns and makes his way through the group of you, and past the guards who have taken up position at the entrance. Without further ado, he disappears into the courtyard beyond.

She appraises you, then sharply raps out orders. “Against the wall light armor over there, medium armor in that corner. Line up in order of height.” The apprentices bundle up the javelins and store them carefully against a wall, and then take out marked lengths of cord and begin measuring you.

“I’ve been instructed to provide you each with any weaponry and non- heavy armor you require. Some of you look well equipped already (she looks at Valron’s House armor), but that insignia needs to go away. Look over the gear once you’ve been measured and we’ll get you equipped. You’ll find that we have all common and martial weapons available, and we can forge anything else.

“Captain Xulleyl is paying for all of the equipment I issue you today, from her own personal funds. If anything is missing, however, it comes from your own personal funds, at five times the cost.”

She looks over at Zacxh appraisingly. “Naturally, you’ll be equipped first.” With a more disparaging glance at the group as a whole, she grumbles to him, “And you’re responsible for this rabble while they’re in my shop.”

Zacxh (not by his own choice is the first to be outfitted in new armor (chain shirt) weapons (twin rapiers) and cloths to suspend his nearly obscene prancing about in a slaves loincloth. (black travelers breaches and high soft boots.) Once adorned, he looks very professional and ready in contrast to his previous Hodge podge and worn attire. While the group, each in their turn is outfitted, Zacxh speaks in low tones with a bemused looking Lt. Ardul. Zacxh gestures several times toward members of the party though never raises his gaze to meet the eyes of the Lieutenant during their 3 minute exchange.

The Lieutenant departs and Zacxh returns to where the group is gathered with their new gear. Once all are finished, he raises his hand to delay your departure and addresses you all with a lowered and distant gaze.

"I have spoken with the Lieutenant and have arranged training for those of you who believe you would benefit from it. We have been granted access to the 'arena' for our martial training and a master in arms will meet us there to administer lessons. I for one am in need of practice. Further, a scout and locksmith will be available to train in the arts of evasion and lock and trap bypassing, and a 'master of the mind' will be available for those of you whose training takes them... inward."

"I saw many varied talents used in the arena though I admit to having been very distracted. I'm sure there are other skill types I have neglected to account for. Upon our return to the barracks, I will sequester my self in my quarters... (a hopeful look to Valron, Zacxh’s roommate for permission)... If anyone has further requirements for trainers please see me and I will make requests to accommodate you. If you doubt my discretion or hold a continuing distain for my service to you, well please feel free to risk your hide by asking the officers yourself or by attempting to self train. I will not take it personally. Otherwise please know that I will strive to respect your privacy. Though personally, I believe that the more we come to know of each other the more effective we can be. Remember my only aim in this is to strengthen the individuals of this unit to make it stronger."

Valron considers Zacxh for a moment and replies,

"Training would indeed be welcome. In addition to improving my skill in fighting, I would also like to practice the art of bathmastery. I approached Lt. Ardul this morning and discovered that there is a bath house nearby but I do not as yet know whether we have access to it. I was told that my request for access outside of our quarters would need to proceed through proper channels. If you would be so good as to inquire on my behalf, it would be appreciated. In addition to helping us gather strength after training sessions, I think we could all use...(he takes a whiff of Zacxh) a good cleansing."

Zacxh does not react in any way to the implication that he stinks, though in fact in his new armor and clothing he mostly emits a slight smell of weapon oil. The slave has been trained to keep himself meticulously clean so that he may better heal between bouts, and be less repulsive to demanding priestesses

"Of course Valron. I will be happy to inquire. I suspect it may be a while before we are given free run of this stronghold, but nonetheless, I will see what I can do. Let be wait if I may, until I have heard the requests of our other companions so that I may be concise and complete in my list of requirements when I next approach our hosts."

"At least we have gained access to the weapons master. That will certainly give us something to chew on until I can beg to round out our training. I look forward to sparring with you. Our techniques are very different and we could learn much from one another I think."

Zacxh bows to Valron in a gesture of compliance, though his typical look of absent defiance is missing.

Kadyel approaches Zacxh after the others have had a word with him.

"I require the services of any fighter. I would also like to hear which others have requested the services of any spellcaster. Can you assist, Appointed One?"

Zacxh bows slightly as Kadyel approaches and awaits her command with the blank and well practiced deference of a well beaten slave. As she speaks he nods his understanding.

"I have been granted use of a master at arms and will announce a schedule very soon for his availabilty. You, however are the first to come with a request for a spellcaster. As I am quite nieve about things arcane, I wonder if some particular school or focus of training would be most helpful for you. Otherwise I will merely request that an arcane spellcaster is availed for your instruction." Zacxh stands motionless, and patiently looks at his feet awaiting further command.

Kadyel grows impatient with the evasive nature of the conversation and visibly scowls.

"Perhaps you misunderstood me. I am not looking for a master of the arcane. Nor do I seek the divine. I seek to find out what spellcasters the others have requested. If there are none, then I seek one of either type. Have all the others spoken with you at this time?"

Trynn stands off to side and does not request any gear or weapons. Instead he spends his time at the armory studying Ardul with unconcealed suspicioun.

Nal examines the contents of the armory while he waits his turn. When Shar comes to him, they exchange a few quiet words before she leads him across the room to look at something. They have what seems to be a short negotiation, during which Shar presents Nal with a few daggers for his consideration. When they finish, Nal looks exceedingly pleased as he walks back to the group. When Shar turns back to face the group and continue her work, she seems momentarily distracted before her familiar hard expression returns.

Inarra strides into the armory and engages in a distracted perusal of the various weapons. She lifts a couple rapiers to swing them about, apparently to test for weight and balance. Her form looks like she might be just now remembering how to use one, she manages not to cut anyone before Shar takes the weapon from her and roughly shoos her away.

Inarra then descends upon the apprentice bowyer Faer (a fairly attractive young male) working in the corner. She handles several bows, stroking them to test their smoothness and flexing their shafts not too unexpertly. A discussion ensues that occasionally leaves the poor young elf blushing and wringing his hands. The conversation ends as Faer gives her a graceful bow, and quicklly returns to his work.

Inarra walks quickly over to Lt. Ardul, and waits respectfully for his notice. In a breif conversation Inarra plainly is requesting something to do with with bowyer as she gestures towards him several times. Ardul looks looks unamused and with raised brows clearly gives her a firm dismissal, and turns away.

Inarra, looking nonplused makes a brief request of the armorer who sizes her up with a glance and makes several markings on a chalk tablet. Looking marginally satistfied she returns to await return to their "quarters."

While waiting for His team to fininsh their business, Zacxh flexes his creaking new gauntlets a few times and loosens his well oiled Rapiers in their shoulder mounded scabbards once more before turning to the door and holding it for the departure of the party. Heholds it in a way which bespeaks years of personal servitude to cruel lords as you all depart.

ChapterZero

CHAPTER 0. THE GREAT ESCAPE

“Crack!... Crack! Crack!” Lucinda’s vicious snake headed whip bit again and again. “Crack” “You ungrateful little bastard! Don’t you even have the sense to cry out. You would deprive your mistress of the pleasure of your song!!! Well, I will see to it that you sing.” “Crack!” Zacxh knew his reaction or, in this case, a lack thereof would have little effect on the outcome of this beating. He had been whipped too many times to be conned by the enraged words of a priestess. She would whip him until either he fell insensible or until she found something else to appease her cruelty. In Lucinda’s case it would probably be the former. She loved to see a male fall victim to her wrath. “Crack, Crack, Crack…” “Scream you insolent bastard!!!” A few years ago he might have even done it. He might have thought that by screaming he would appease her in some way. It could work on mistress Serinill, maybe on Mistress Theria too. But this Lucinda, well she was a real piece of work. His only defense would be his inevitable weakness. Therein lay the problem. His weakness was beginning to fail him. His body had grown large and tough it is true, but that was not it. Larger more formidable males would have collapsed by now. Zacxh had found a ‘hiding spot’ in his mind. It was strange, and in a way he knew it had been there all along, but now he could run there and take shelter at will. He used to feel a great sense of despair and loss when his body was beaten and deformed. It was just that attachment that had concealed the hiding spot from him. He now knew that his body was not related to his mind, but was simply its vehicle. Today His vehicle was going to be beaten into a bloody rag. “Crack” “Fall you insolent pig” Zacxh could hear the Snake headed whip. He could, in a detached way, feel the painful neurotoxin of the vipers' every bite. But the pain lived in his nerves and his brain. It no longer penetrated his mind. Unfortunately, that meant that his battered, branded, tattooed, and pierced frame would have to fend for itself. Loss of blood and shock would eventually bring it down, though it would take a while. This was not pleasing to the Mistress. Actually she had found other more satisfying subjects for her pleasure, and seemed almost apathetic and mechanical in her abuse. “Crack!” “I will flay your flesh and feed it to the worgs you insolent pig, now cry out your devotion to me or DIE!!!” Zacxh smiled instead. He found it sad and slightly amusing that she was so disinterested in his torture that she had called him ‘pig” again. She had definitely lost interest. It hadn’t always been that way. For a time, he had even been favored by the priestess of House Oussund. They had utterly destroyed his family in a raid to raise the status of their house. He was so young then. Barely even a boy. He had been born into the role of Guard-leader aspirant, and had his house survived, he would have had an entire section under his command. He would have been killing priestesses in routine raids and watching *them* cry out for mercy. Ah well. His lot was not so bad. In fact, he had recently come to appreciate his position. He was a pit fighter; an anonymous champion of House Oussund. As such, great care was taken to ensure he was as prepared as possible for his next bout. As a child he had learned to pounce on other boys... and orcs and lizard folk quickly and quietly. He knew just where to slide his knife to still a beating heart or disable a troublesome sword arm. He proved an able and recorseful fighter and had killed off all his kin in the first year or so of his enslavement. He was strong, cunning and quick in combat and thus proved to be of great value to House Oussund. Like any prize, they kept him in good repair, or at least fully functional. His missing digits were painfully and grudgingly replaced by chiding priestesses who beat him senseless with clubs and whips for the favor. His right ear was but a tattered rag and his ebony skin was so stitched with grey scars that it was difficult, in some areas, to find any virgin flesh at all. His knuckles were thick and knobby from repeated breaking and his nose was flat and round like an orc’s. His tattoos and marks of ownership were all but indiscernible anymore, lost in the tattered menagerie of his flesh Yes, She would beat him into a pulpy, bloody wreck. Then he would be salved and stitched up by some servant and left to his fevers and dementias. He would lie in a painful ball for days or weeks and would eventually come to his senses. Then a bout. Would it be a beast again? Maybe a young troll? He would be given a spear or sword, sometimes a net or sharpened stick. He would be cast into darkness or blinding, painful light and shoved into some cramped space to fight to the death. Then, as a reward for victory, he would be forced to couple with some priestess or another who would chastise and goad him for his lack of enthusiasm then proceed to beat him again into a bleeding, retching, discarded heap of flesh. It was an endless cycle and Zacxh knew it would eventually end in death. Zacxh had grown accustomed to the savage cycle of victory, punishment and reward and had actually begun to look forward to his fights, but now he knew he was in danger. His lack of care for his body’s wellbeing was beginning to show, and so he no longer was of use to the priestesses of Loth. He would soon be sold to the mines or, perhaps, tortured to death or sacrificed in some way. He knew his end was near. Zacxh surmised that the most likely form of his demise would be some skilled or overpowering adversary in the pit. His priestesses would drug or disable him in some way and bet heavily against his victory. He had been so sucessful in the pit, that they could easily make a heafty profit from his defeat. Perhaps, he thought, his time was at hand. He had heard whisperings that he was to be wrapped in leather armor, masked to disguise his wounds, and sent into the pit against Gruulosh, the renowned and reportedly unbeatable champion of another house. If true, He was doomed. His arms and legs were hanging limp and near lifeless. Even the dangerous venom of a green mobeus spider would barely stimulate him enough to walk. He could perhaps muster enough strength to feebly clutch his spear and drag himself about, but there would be no power in him. Yes, Zacxh thought, at long last, this was probably going to be his fated day. So lost in his conjecture was Zacxh, that he barely noticed, when the beating stopped. Where had Lucinda gone? He pulled himself up and found that the door to the arena was not open, and there were no weapons or armor about. Perhaps he would not fight today. Instead, the passage to the observing deck lay open. Was he meant to climb the stair and watch a bout? He struggled with the idea a moment. He had never watched one before, but soon crept up to a private observation booth. No one would see him here and there was a note addressed to him on the seat...

Two combatants entered the small private arena. All around were other discreet observation booths shrouded in darkness. How many hidden Elves were watching? One of the combatants was a large and only slightly drugged ogre. The other had the same build and stance as Zacxh. Both warriors were armed with small sharp pikes and masked to hide their faces. The elf was scarred and torn of body and watching him was like looking in a reflecting pool. The combat was short. The Dark elf died on the ogre’s pike after only a single failed parry. Zacxh sighed and opened the note...

Zacxh wasted no time leaving the arena. He knew the twisting hallways which wound out of house Ossund, but since his childhood eighty some years hence he had never followed them all the way through to the door.. He reread his note. Without giving a reason, It instructed him to leave in secrecy and meet a caravan, but getting to the crystal gate would be no easy task. He was a secret slave of house Ossund, not meant to be wandering the halls, and worse yet, he was presumed dead. Perhaps, he thought, he should try to escape via the service exit near the kitchen. He noted wryly that he was unarmed and wearing only his soft boots and a bloodstained loincloth. Zacxh clung to seldom used corridors with his torn ears tuned to every possible source of danger. Several times he had to dive into a side chamber or hide in a tight corner to avoid discovery. By the time he reached the kitchens he was shaking with tension. A few servants were working to prepare the middle meal for some house guards. They did not notice as Zacxh stole quietly into their presence. He crammed his body into a tight space between a scalding hot oven and a prep table. The oven toasted his flesh slightly as he waited and watched the comings and goings of the kitchen staff. He could not be discovered, so he waited until there was a break between servings. When only one Servant remained and was immersed in the task of washing pots, Zacxh made his escape. He grabbed a sturdy looking kitchen knife, and slipped out the delivery door. Zacxh stopped outside the kitchen long enough to dig through a trash bin. He dug out an old filthy cloak and a tired leather belt into which he tucked his fine carving knife. The cloak had a hood and, though ill fitting of his pit fighter's war shaped frame, it concealed his scarred and tattooed skin. He had little trouble, thus adorned, blending into the traffic which would conceil his passage through the crystal gate. True to the prediction of the mysterious scroll, there was a caravan in need of laborers making for Nerr'tenden. A stern and impatient looking caravan leader tapped her foot and rolled her eyes despairingly at Zacxh's approach. As the caravan made preparations to leave, two other outsiders joined the group. The one who tersly introduced himself as Nal, was a handsome but tight lipped elf adorned in Fine black traveling cloths and a wearing creepy black short blade. The pommel was decorated with a set of clenched teeth which seemed to grip the blade. The overall effect of his good looks, cruel eyes, and macobre choice of armament was definately disturbing. The other, Valron, was a strong, well groomed Fighter wearing the uniform of a house guard. He carried a large wicked looking trident, and his body language was loose and comfortable. He carried his weapon with a careless ease which bespoke a deadly familiarity. In Valron, Zacxh's experienced eye beheld a formidable warrior. The caravan guards ignored the newcomers for the most part, though as they made final preparations, Rath, the caravan's leader, addressed them curtly. She concisely told them that they were expected to pay for their own rations and carry their own weight. She informed them that she was only allowing for their presence on the off chance they might prove useful as fodder in any unforeseen skirmishes which may lay ahead. Zacxh merely nodded his head at the instructions and tried to keep out of the way as the caravan finally moved out. The ominous well dressed traveler kept to himself for the most part. The well groomed fighter spoke a bit with the guards and toyed with a bandoleer of small vials hanging across his chest. Zacxh stayed near a line of chained dueagar slaves who shuffled along bearing gear and cargo. For the first few days the caravan moved along the Underdark with good speed and in relative safety. Rath made several stops at increasingly small outposts picking up supplies and making deliveries. One town (?), several days into the trek, was famous for tea. Rath allowed a night for the travelers to enjoy a relaxing and highly traditional tea ceremony and a good meal. Zacxh traded his only valuable possession, the fine kitchen knife to a sour faced cook for a poor pot of thin stew and a rusted and dull dagger with a greasy and worn scabbard. Still the weapon had a nice balance and after countless hours of rubbing and scraping, it cleaned up well enough to be serviceable. Rath provided sparse rations to her crew as they continued generally north. Both of the other newcomers, the creepy eyed dandy and the wellspoken guard, seemed a bit put off by the cheap rations, but to Zacxh each meal was a feast. Whatever the scriber of the note had in store, these days were a happy time. Freedom from the house walls, plentiful food and tea... It was a long overdue turn of fate. Zacxh looked down at his heavily scarred arms and hands. They were an ugly reminder of the careless cruelty that even now Zacxh was beginning to purge from his mind. All that pain, anger and viciousness was leaving his conscious mind and taking up residence... somewhere else. He wondered if someday it might rear up and manifest itself in some physical way. Certainly he had scars. Noble Valron made several friendly remarks to Zacxh and seemed generally personable but Nal, the dark brooding elf kept mostly to himself. For his part, Zacxh lied that he was a servant performing a menial errand for his house and tried to avoid saying anything which might betray the fact that he was in fact, an escaped slave and fugitive. After days of rapid travel, the group entered some seldom used backwater caverns which were reportedly a 'shortcut' toward Nerr’tenden. Eventually, after a number of turns and twists that left Zacxh completely disoriented, they happened upon a slaughtered caravan. The bodies of a dozen or so guards were strewn into a shallow uncovered grave. As (?) the scout pushed ahead to look for an ambush, Zacxh pillaged the dead for scraps of workable armor and weapons. He quickly strapped on a mismatched suit consisting of Leather greaves and gauntlets, a boiled leather jerkin and bloodied bracers. He found two decent long thin blades and strapped them, crossing, to his back. He also found a nice hand crossbow and set a short quiver of bolts on his left hip. He replaced the scabbard but kept his own dagger. It had finally come to a fine edge and was Zacxh's first real possession in the world. As an afterthought, Zacxh collected up a few coins and a small pouch to put them in, ignoring the disgusted faces of his traveling companions. They were the first coins he had owned in eighty some years. Zacxh emerged from the shallow pit armed, wealthy, and happy. For the first time in ages he felt free. He was elated, and most surprising, was eager for the fight ahead. He was armed, by choice this time, and if he were to fight, he enjoyed the prospect of a true victory, not one sullied by drugging, poor equipment, or other underhanded tampering. Just as Zacxh was tightening the last straps of his armor, (scout) the scout returned with news of an ambush ahead. He led the guards down a side hallway and as Zacxh, Valron and Nal made to follow, Rath quickly deputized them and admonished them to 'Stay out of the way and not do anything stupid.' Zacxh had seldom heard less needed advice. (scout) led the way, pushing about fifty feet ahead. He poked his head around a turn in the naturally formed stone and, seeing no threat, stepped around. The sound of four crossbow strings heralded the arrival of well aimed bolts which jerked and slammed (scout's) body. A gout of greenish foam erupted from his mouth as he fell lifeless to the floor. The guards seemed shocked and confused a moment, so Zacxh acted first. He remembered an old elf trick a fellow slave had taught him and brought a deepened darkness about the fallen scout. Then, taking advantage of the gloomy cover, Zacxh pulled (scout) back around the corner and out of the line of fire. More bolts were fired blindly into the darkness but they merely clacked ineffectually on the stone around them. Zacxh took a quick look at (scout) and realized he was beyond help. The green ooze dribbling from the jovial elf's lips spelled doom. Zacxh emptied his thoughts and let himself slip into the 'hidden place' in his mind. He became a being beyond pain. His senses became detached and super acute, and he became so attuned to the movement and forces around himself that he felt he could 'see' right into the most vital spots of those around him. The places on their bodies where their energies converged. Zacxh charged... And, as he broke free of the globe of darkness, found himself joined by Guards Valron and Nal. Only the slaves and a pair of attending guards had stayed behind. The melee lasted only a moment. Zacxh and Valron quickly dispatched a pair of ambushers and the guards fightin allongside nal Nal felled the other two, yet this was merely a delaying force. The chamber narrowed and led around another bend. Zacxh and the guards joined Rath and entered a large circular chamber. It seemed empty and anticlimactic. One of the guards motioned to the south wall indicating the presence of some suspicious looking cracks. Zacxh, two guards and Rath went over to have a look and were suddenly caught in the thick sticky strands of a spell web. Crossbow bolts flew 'through' the northern wall, and with them came the realization that the wall was illusory, merely a trick of magic, perspective and the dim shadows of photo luminescent fungi. Three figures were concealed by that wall. Two fired hand crossbows into the captive guards and one was preparing another incantation like the one which had created the webs. Zacxh struggled in vain to force his way free of his entanglement while watching Valron ram her trident lethally onto one of the crossbowman. The mage finished his incantation and vanished from view at about the same moment Zacxh finally tore free of the webs and partially dodged a hastily aimed bolt. The tiny, likely poisoned missile managed to nick his side as it deflected off his boiled leather breastplate. Zacxh never noticed his slight wound, and drove the point of his rapier into the belly of the remaining crossbowman. The doomed elf scooped at his spilling guts and crumpled to the ground as all the color drained from his face. Nal called out "Valron come to me and we will block the escape. Let the others flush him out. All sound stopped and the party collectively held their breath listening for some sign of the illusive mage. "Infernus arachnidious!" The mage popped back into view as a blindingly bright fan of flames leapt from his splayed fingers and into the guardsmen still trapped in the thick sticky strands of the web. "FOOF!" The webs caught aflame and instantly went up in a smoky greasy explosion of heat. Rath dove free of the worst of the flames, but both the male guards shreaked horribly as flesh dripped molten off of their faces and limbs. They died screaming and curling into blackened, gory horrors. Rath, Zacxh and Nal descended upon the murdering mage with the fury of a cave in. Blows came from all sides and it was only a moment before the mage was trussed and tied to a pole. Nal seemed to relish his cruel interrogation of the prisoner and Zach left him to the grisly work in order to search the cave. Zacxh poked around the cave looking for whatever could have put these brigands into such a defensive posture. He found two large sacks in the corner and was struck momentarily speechless as he discovered they contained a huge fortune in Semi cut rubies. Many were nearly priceless, as large as a fist. "Hey Rath, we have a situation here... " Zacxh wanted to be wealthy just as well as the next, but all but two of the guards were dead. The chest was large, and they were still a good couple days of travel from Nerr’tenden. This cache of wealth meant pursuit and suspicion and untold danger. Even worse, Rath explained that the rubies were identifiably cut and marked with the symbol of the House Godendar ruby mines at Tleth'tyrr. Trouble. Whoever turned up with this treasure would likely not live long enough to spend it The diminished party of six warriors and the six slaves set out soon thereafter. They shortened the shackles of the Dueagar and loaded them with a gagged and bound mage as well as an unbelievable treasure in rubies. Zacxh persuaded Rath to lend him (scouts) enchanted cloak of concealment and used it to scout ahead of the vulnerable convoy for trouble. The caravan move quickly and only stopped often enough to keep the slaves from dying from exhaustion in their boots. As Rath feared, the deep dwarves could not resist the temptation of all those rubies. All but two, as well as one of Rath”s trusted guards died when the hopeless bastards tried to make their escape. The remaining two were assigned to carry the captive mage. The caravan which rolled to the gates of Nerr’tenden was but a shadow of the one which departed the Crystal Gate. A guard and an officer greeted the ragged band as they approached the gate. The officer wore a 'spider pin'. Zacxh was relieved to be done with the poorly run caravan and never looked back as he walked straight up to the lieutenant and presented him with the stone token he received with his note. It was accepted silently. Valron and Nal walked up and each produced similar stones. They were taken. The lieutenant seemed amused by the haggard looking caravan and after only a moment led the way into a heavily fortified keep. He tersly introduced himself as 'Lieutenant Ardul' and seemed ungrateful for the rubies which, as a token of good faith and to be rid of their inherent danger, Rath at the advice of Zacxh, Valron and Nal gifted to house Oussund. He said they would bring nothing but trouble as they were ransomed back to their rightful owners. He sequestered the guard and Rath in a separate room, and made it fairly clear that they would not live to see another day. Zacxh Valron and Nal were brought to a small barracks chamber and locked in. Apparently they had found their new home. Nal bunked alone in one of the double rooms, and Valron and Zacxh took a room together. It looked like there was room for eight in the squad bay, and it seemed to Zacxh that he could trust the former Oussund house guard to watch his back. At least they had shared the road together, and they shared a confidence in the secret of the rubies. He seemed a quiet but steady enough roommate. The Lieutenant came in awhile later. He apprised the trio of travelers warily before speaking. "Well it seems you were able to arrive in one piece which is more than can be said for the balance of your caravan... You should choose quarters and settle in. The rest will arrive soon..." With that, he tossed each of the three a large ruby in the rough. They were cut only enough to transport to skilled shapers but each bore the inscription of hoise godendor. "Let these be a reminder to you of your trials along the road and of the danger you faced in taking that treasure. You were right to give them up as they are a political hot potato and would surely have burnt you had you opted to fence them yourself. The less said of them, the better.'

The lieutenant left without further ado.

Another Scarred Elf arrived a few hours later. He was blindfolded and exhibited the abused marks of a slave. He introduced himself as Trynn but said little else.

(from e-mail) Zacxh is sitting cross legged in a cramped and uncomfortable corner Rubbing the rust and grime off of his well used looking pair of rapiers with a handful of sand. He has mended his well used leather armor and seems content to work mindlessly hour after hour on his gear to bring it to its highest possible level of readiness. His only piece of clothing that does not seem battered and mended is his dark, flat black cloak.

Zacxh Looks up at the newcomer with dead expressionless eyes, and his heavily battered and scarred face cracks into a slight grin, though his eyes still seem dead.

"We seem to have been inducted as servants of some sort into a new house. I for one was invited to come and did so willingly to escape certain death at the hands of my priestesses."

"My name is Zacxh..." (pronounced Zak-Sh)"and I am at your service"

"The fact that you have been thrown in with us seems... unfortunate for you. We seem to be forming a scouting party of some sort, and will doubtless be soon dead. Hand me your blade and I will be happy to clean it for you. As you can see mine are nearly finished. If it is well maintained, perhaps you might thrust it into an enemy before you die"

Zacxh returns his attention to a bit of stubborn rust and seems to lose interest in the newcomer. The slight grin fades. Forgotten. (end email)

By twos and threes, the remaining four members of 'The Barracks' arrived. They were: Sorn a handsome male dancer lightly armed, Inarra a gorgeous and aloof debutant with a distain for all the lesser 'Little People' in the room, Kadyel A huge tough looking female warrior, Len we, A lightly armored and quiet male. Introductions were made, and it was immediately apparent that the there were three classes of elf in the room. The slaves, the privileged, and the aloof. Normally, Zacxh would have gravitated to Trynn as slaves will often do, but there was something shifty and sinister about the tough looking brawler which turned Zacxh away. Sorn the dancer seemed the friendliest of the lot but plied his attentions primarily upon Inarra. Len we was quiet and watchful and Kadyel held slaves in obvious distain seeming to Zacxh a typical female hard case. Zacxh surveyed the room one last time and decided that his choice of Valron as a bunkmate was his best bet of not being killed as he rested. Hours passed, and people had felt each other out a bit when food arrived by armed guard. The atmosphere felt more like a prison than a barracks.

Zacxh smiled instead. He found it sad and slightly amusing that she was so disinterested in his torture that she had called him ‘pig” again. She had definitely lost interest.

It wasn’t always this way. For a time, he had actually even been favored by the priestess of House Oussund. They had utterly destroyed his family in a raid thereby raising the status of their house. He was so young then. Barely even a boy. He had been born into the role of Guard-leader aspirant. Had his house survived, he would have an entire section under his command even now. He would have been killing priestesses in routine raids and watching *them* cry out for mercy. Ah well. His lot was not so bad.

He had recently come to appreciate his position. He was a pit fighter, and a champion of House Oussund. As such, great care was taken to ensure he was as prepared as possible for his next bout. As a child he had learned to pounce on other boys and orcs and lizard folk quickly and quietly. He knew just where to slide his knife to still a beating heart or disable a troublesome sword arm. He had killed off all his kin in the first year or so of his enslavement. He was strong cunning and quick in combat and thus proved to House Oussund his worth.

Like any prize they kept him in good repair, or at least fully functional. His missing digits were painfully and grudgingly replaced by chiding priestesses who beat him senseless with clubs and whips for the favor. His right ear was a tattered rag and his ebony skin was so stitched with grey scars that it was difficult in some areas to find any virgin flesh at all. His knuckles were thick and knobby from repeated breaking and his nose was flat and round like an orc’s. His tattoos and marks of ownership were all but indiscernible anymore, lost in the tattered menagerie of his flesh

Yes, She would beat him into a pulpy pile of goop. Then he would be salved and stitched up by some servant and left to his fevers and dementias. He would lie in a painful ball for days or weeks and would eventually come to his senses. Then a bout. Would it be a beast again? Maybe a young troll. He would be given a spear or sword, sometimes a net or sharpened stick. He would be cast into darkness or blindingly painful light and shoved into some cramped space to fight to the death. Then, as a reward for victory he would be forced to couple with some priestess or another who would chastise and goad him for his lack of enthusiasm then proceed to beat him again into a bleeding retching pile of goo. It was an endless cycle and would eventually end in death. Zacxh had grown accustomed to the cycle and had actually begun to look forward to his fights, but now he knew he was in danger. His lack of care for his body’s wellbeing was beginning to become apparent and so he no longer was of use to the priestesses of Loth. He would soon be sold to the mines or tortured to death or sacrificed in some way. He knew his end was near. The most likely form of his demise would be some skilled of overpowering adversary in the pit. His priestesses would drug or disable him in some way and bet heavily against his victory.

Perhaps today would be that day. He had heard whisperings that he was to be wrapped in leather armor and masked to disguise his wounds and sent into the pit against a renowned champion of another house. If true, He was doomed. His arms and legs were hanging limp and near lifeless. Even the dangerous venom of a green mobeus spider would barely stimulate him enough to walk. He would clutch his spear and drag himself about, but there would be no strength. Yes, at long last, this was probably going to be the day.

Zacxh had barely noticed, but the beating had stopped. Where had everyone gone? He pulled himself up and found that the door to the arena was not open. He would not fight today. Instead, the passage to the observing deck lay open. He was meant to watch a bout? He struggled with the idea a moment as he had never watched one before, but soon crept up the stairs to a private observation booth. No one would see him here and there was a not addressed to him on the seat.

Two combatants entered small private arena. All around were other observation booths shrouded in darkness. How many Dark Elves were watching. One of the combatants was a large and only slightly drugged ogre the other had the same build and stance as Zacxh. Both warriors were armed with small sharp pikes and maked to hide their faces. The elf was scarred and torn of body and watching him was like looking in a reflecting pool.

The combat was short. The Dark elf died on the ogre’s pike after only a single failed parry. Zacxh opened the note.

last edited 2005-11-11 08:12:14 by Cliff

CharacterSheets

Character Sheet Resources

There are a ton of character sheets out there, including user-fillable PDF forms. Some even perform calculations. Here are some of my favorites:

Excel Based

The Hero Forge and Spell Forge sheets on the Yahoo SpiderGuard Groups page are huge and cumbersome but they yield good results. (I've figured out how to modify them to make a gestalt rules character, and I'm happy to help out with that for your character. -Eric)

Fillable PDF

You need the Professional version of Adobe Acrobat to save filled-out PDF forms, but anyone with Acrobat Reader can fill one out and print it.

  • The Hypertext d20 SRD site has a pretty modern looking PDF character sheet that performs calculations where possible. They also have an already filled-out example.

  • The Mad Irishman has one to check out.

Plain Old PDF

  • Wizards of the Coast has a number of character sheets available, with more than a few for specific character classes.

  • The Hypertext d20 SRD site also offers a plain-Jane, non-fillable PDF version.

last edited 2005-11-09 21:35:33 by Eric

City Council

The most powerful eight houses of each city send their Matriarch to be part of the City Council. The Council typically strives to maintain city order (as they choose to see it) through diplomacy, intimidation, trade restrictions and military might. Note that there are no "city" resources - each Matriarch can only commit its own resources to Council activities. This can cause complications...

last edited 2005-09-20 19:20:54 by Steve

Cleric

PC's can't be clerics in this campaign, as this is a highly restrictive class to play. Only females can be clerics, and only clerics of Lolth are sanctioned in this society.

Females who do become clerics of the Spidery Queen aren't good matches for gaming because they are extremely restricted in their activities - they spend the vast majority of their time either governing and making policy decisions or keeping non-clerics in line with proper respect for Her.

Clerics pretty much have their time cut out for them and that's the way it is.

last edited 2005-09-23 15:47:25 by Steve

Clues

This is a place for stray bits of knowledge and clues that you come across.

From Zacxh:

The old mining foreman was very trusted by the miners and knowledgable. She retired, and was replaced by an incompetent and paranoid buffoon *just* before the cave ins. (the new foreman is a cousin of Lt. Ardul)

The poison in the shipment was not suited to attacking a water supply.

The forecasted tunnels on the infiltrator maps lead toward the eight pointed symbol. None reach them yet.

Could it be related that a large shipment of rubies recently went missing?

The first contingent of gaurds that Valron and Zacxh encountered on their first foray into the mines (one day before the main party) wore an alternating mix of house Oussund uniforms and stealthy rogue type outfits.

The body with no blood and a happy look on its face had no visible wounds, (or bite marks that Zacxh or Valron could find) and was discovered just outside the cave-in near the secret entrance. He was not recognized by any of the 'regular' miners and was dressed in rogue wear with a cloth-silenced shortsword.

There was a spy who Zacxh and Valron brought to Captain Xulleyl. The spy was named Jhul (Like 'Jewell'). Captain X asked Zacxh to get him quickly and bring him to her. We abducted him from the chowhall and dragged him unconcious to the Captain's quarters. He was a member of Lt. Ardul's troop. (The Lt. was not pleased that we were screwing with his men without his permission). Captain X showed the spy a note (possibly the one from Sorn's pocket???) and when Jhul reacted in fear, Captain X decapitated him on the spot. We departed immediately to come find you (and kill a few dozen cave dwellers allong the way.)

cave death toll (edited by Kadyel):

  • 2 mages

  • 1 captain

  • 2 sergeant

  • 2 high level scout type attendants with one of the mages.

  • several dozen green troops (poor tactics...) Kadyel: maybe 28 total? Someone who didn't miss a session is a better person to estimate than me...

There is a powerful opposing mage running around melting the walls.

Any enemy of them is a .... To us?

Lt Ardul took the vast haul of recovered rubies from Zacxh, Valron, and Nal upon their arrival to Nertenden. It was later discovered that he did not report the treasure to The Captain. This occured several weeks before the mine incident. Coincidence???

Lt. Ardul seems central to many of the happenings in the mines.

His cousin was forman during the cave in.

His trooper was a spy (Jhull).

He took the rubies for himself(did not inform the Captain of them).

He has been forbidden to work with the spidergaurd.

Also, the poison in "family sized" portions is contact poison.

The eight pointed symbol is not an indicator of one particular item, but more like a resource that is found in a few spots, or even a vein...

Bandits similar to our late friends from the mines appear to have siezed a shipment of Godendar rubies some weeks ago. Perhaps the symbols are positions of Oussund sapphire deposits or even Godendar's ruby veins and someone is attempting to purloin the wealth of one or both of these houses.

DarkStarlet

Dark starlets represent the ultimate expression of the darker side of fame. They seek to use their spells and abilities to control and manipulate their audience solely to enhance their fame and dominance in life and their art. They can be haughty and arrogant to those they deem "below them" (anyone they have ever successfully intimidated or manipulated) and flattering and beguiling to their "betters" (anyone they haven't dominated yet or could improve their the starlet's status).

Inspiration: "When you're a beautiful supermodel and have millions of dollars, it's almost your obligation to destroy the lives of the ugly poor people around you." Maybe a darker version of The Charmer

Skill Points at Each Level 4 + Int modifier.

Class Features

Distracting Presence

Due to their glamorous nature and dazzling aspect, Dark Starlets gain their Charisma bonus to their AC. They retain this bonus when flat footed. Though they loose this bonus if they are concealed from the attacker or behind cover.

Starlet Nature

Dark Starlets gain a bonus to diplomacy skill checks equal to their class level when dealing with their "betters", and a penalty to their diplomacy skill checks equal to their class level when deal with "the little people."

The converse is also true for intimidate skill checks, they get an equivalent bonus when dealing with "underlings" and a penalty when dealing with "patrons."

Charmed Performance

[Not sure how to work this, the idea is that the starlet would get a bonus to their resist DC to Enchantment(Charm) or Telepathy (Charm) spells or powers based upon their ranks in a perform skill, or perhaps a perform skill check result. The spell would have to be cast within X rounds of the performance?]

Compelling Performance

Similar to above but for Enchantment(compulsion) or Telepathy (compulsion) spells

Dark Charmer

Members of this prestige class are suffused with charm, allure, and presence. What the world does not see however, is the need to dominate, control and manipulate everything and everyone. And should those 'delicate' tactics fail, kill that which cannot be mastered, most often by the subtle use of poison. No sneak attacks in the dark for these folks. When you die it will be looking into their eyes, confused and surprised at the betrayal, and should the charmer be good enough, maybe even glad that their radiant face was the last thing you saw.

Based loosely on the Charmer prestige class http://www.hallofhero.com/PC/ViewPressClass.cfm?IDPC=61 and the Assassin Prestige class http://d20srd.org/srd/prestigeClasses/assassin.htm

Hit Die

d6

Requirements

To qualify to become a dark charmer, a character must fulfill all the following criteria

Abilities

Charisma 18+

Skills

Diplomacy 8 Ranks, Intimidate 8 ranks

Spells/Powers

Ability to cast/manifest at least three spells from the school of enchantment/telepathy. At least one of these spells must be 3rd level or higher.

Special

The character must kill someone outside of melee using poison and the victim must know who did it.

Class Skills

Bluff (Cha), Concentration (Con), Craft (Int), Decipher Script (Int), Diplomacy (Cha), Disguise (Cha), Forgery (Int), Gather Information (Cha), Intimidate (Cha), Knowledge (all skills, taken individually), Listen (Wis), Perform (Cha), Profession (Wis), Sense Motive (Wis), Sleight of Hand (Dex), and Spot (Wis). Psicraft* (Int) OR Spellcraft (Int) (as caster/manifester base class)

Class Features

Weapon and Armor Proficiency

Charmers gain no additional proficiency in any weapon or armor.

Social Grace (Ex)

The Charmer gains a bonus to the skill diplomacy equal to his charmer level.

Poison Use

Dark Charmers are trained in the use of poison and never risk accidentally poisoning themselves when sliding a poisoned needle into someone's wrist, or swabbing contact poison across the back of a lovers neck (you get the point), oh yeah and putting it on blades too, etc.

Trustworthy (Ex)

As per the Trustworthy feat from Song and Silence (+2 bonus on all Diplomacy and Gather Information checks)

How Charming (Ex)

Beginning at 2nd level, the Dark Charmer becomes so charming, it becomes harder to resist his enchantment/telepathy spells/powers. The save DC for any enchantment/telepathy spell/power increases +1. This rises to +2 at 5th level and +3 at 8th level. These increases are cumulative with those granted by the Spell Focus and Greater Spell Focus feats, or their psionic equivalents.

Immune to Charms (Ex)

A Charmer of 2nd level or higher gains immunity to all charm spells and effects and powers. This does not include compulsions.

Arcane Grace (Ex)

The Charmer gains his Charisma bonus to all saving throws. 

Awe Inspiring (Ex) - deleting, replacing with Arcane Grace from 1st level

At 3rd level, a Charmer gains the ability to generate an intangible, invisible aura of awe that overwhelms hostile creatures within a 20-foot radius. Anyone about to attack the Charmer must attempt a Will save (DC = the Charmer's character level + charisma modifier). Those who fail the saving throw suffer a -2 morale penalty to attacks, checks, and save for one fully day or until they successfully damage the charmer generating the aura. A creature that made its initial save or damaged the charmer is immune to this aspect of the Charmer's aura for one day. Charmers ignore the aura of other charmers.

Persuasive (Ex)

As per the Persuasive feat from Song and Silence (+2 bonus on all Bluff checks and Intimidate checks)

Arcane Presence (Su)

The Charmer permanently gains two points to charisma.

Distracting Presence

Due to their alluring nature and charmed aspect, Dark Charmers gain their Charisma bonus to their AC. They retain this even when they would normally loose their Dexterity bonus (e.g. when flat footed). They loose this bonus if they are concealed from the attacker or behind cover. They also loose this bouns if they should wear armor heavier than light. 

 Fascinating (Sp) - deleting, replacing with Distracting Presence

The Charmer may cast mass suggestion once per day as a spell-like ability using his total class level to determine the caster level.

Gilded Tongue (Ex)

A Charmer of 7th level or above can speak with any living creature.

Alluring (Ex)

+2 bonus to Diplomacy and to the DCs of your mind-affecting language-dependant spells (requires Trustworthy, Persuasive and CHA 13+)

Speak the Truth (Su)

One of the Charmer's most powerful abilities: his or her aura so overwhelms others that they find it impossible to lie within the Charmer's presence. This effect is usable to a number of times per day equal to the Charmer's Charisma modifier. The effect has a duration of one minute per character level.

A True Charmer (Ex)

The Charmer uses a new table to determine NPC attitudes, which supersedes Table 5-4 in the DMG.

Other Feature ideas

Trying to think of something darker to replace the higher level class features

A Quick Escape - to replace Gilded Tongue?

Killing people up close so often necessitates an expeditious escape. The Dark Charmer may cast/manifest Dimension Door (psionic or magic as appropriate) 1/day as a free action. This is at their current caster/manifester level. (Similar to the Elocater 3rd level power, and the Master Diplomat prestige class)

Undetectable Lie - to replace Speak the Truth?

One of the Dark Charmer's most powerful abilities. His or her aura so overwhelms others that they find it impossible to detect when the Charmer is lying to them. This effect protects against such spells as Discern Lies, Zone of Truth, special abilities, and during such spells as Read Thoughts, Mind Probe and Probe Thoughts, where the charmer is forced to answer a question, they must answer but they can lie. This effect is usable to a number of times per day equal to the Charmer's Charisma modifier. The effect has a duration of one minute per character level. The Dark Charmer also recieves a +10 on Bluff checks opposed by Sense Motive checks (reverse of Inquisitor feat).

Precision poisoner - to replace True Charmer?

The Dark Charmer's poison use and precision placement reach a synergistic apex. Anytime the dark charmer uses poison against an individual outside of melee, scores a critical hit in melee or executes a coup de grace with a poisoned object, the target must make two savings throws for each damage phase. If either save fails the target suffers the poison's damage.

  • (From the Dark Blade prestige class in the Poisoncraft handbook)

Dinlin

Dinlin Oussund is a cleric of the Spider Queen, and has been assigned to Nerr'tenden.

The residents at the outpost cower from her unpredictable, iron hand and her whip. She spends most of her time either praying to Lolth or stalking the passages and chambers away from the stronghold’s walls. When she isn’t doing one of these things, she is likely berating or whipping one of the stronghold’s inhabitants.

Recently presumed deceased under mysterious circumstances, Dinlin's disappearance has sparked quite a fervor among the clergy.

last edited 2007-11-28 19:47:13 by Andrew

Dolthgurdar

Dolthgurdar is the regional capital and marketplace for a region roughly 100 miles across (as the umber hulk burrows). It is home to roughly fifty noble houses, and is headquarters for all of them. The city is managed by the City Council, whose members adjudicate disputes and make policy decisions.

Its three enormous gates are open for a steady stream of trade that comes in from the entire region.

The First House of the city, House Godendar, guards the city gates and oversees the enormous complexity of trade caravans, markets and disputes that come along with such an active marketplace.

House Oussund is the 28th House of the city.

last edited 2005-09-20 20:22:56 by Steve

Double Agents

The documents found in the mine led Captain Xulleyl to confirm that House Orlylyl appears to have been behind the invasions of the mines at Nerr'tenden. After Falt revealed Valron's identity as an Orlylyl noble, the party decided to attempt a double-agent role with Orlylyl.

Valron wrote a message to send to Valron's Mom, a High Priestess in Orlylyl. Here's what was sent: Valron's Message

The party was barely able to get to Erlynden for a secret meeting with Valron's Sister, where his mother showed up, listened to the full report of happenings in the mines, instructed Valron to 'get the mineral' and then gave a bag of diamonds to pay for the operations.

last edited 2006-03-30 13:54:22 by Steve

Drezen

Drezen is a fungus. It is the primary ingredient in the poison that is commonly used to incapacitate or render unconcious enemies of the dark elves. It's cultivation is generally a house endeavor, as the 'resources' needed to cultivate it seem to be in short supply (though specifics seldom leave the house), this makes Drezen a moderately precious commodity.

Dark elves are immune to the effects of the Drezen fungus.

Editing FAQ

Changing Stuff on this Site:

Creating your Account:

1. Go to http://underwiki.redwoodrhino.com/cgi-bin/moin-1.3.4.cgi/UserPreferences

2. Click 'Create Account' and not login the first time you enter the site, and must fill out all fields. On subsequent logins you need only fill in use and password and click login.

3. Use just your first name in proper case: Nate, Barrett (not nate, barrett)

Then you're in: You home page will be visible on the right as a link with your name.

There are a couple of things you can do to a page: edit one or create one.

To make a page private so only you (and the mighty Steve) can view or edit it, at the top of the page place: 

#acl YourName:read,write,admin,rename,delete

Episodes

The Invitation note that announced the beginning of the campaign.

Very brief summaries of the Spider Guard's adventures so far:

0. Homeward Bound in which the characters travel from Dolthgurdar to Nerr'tenden.

1. First Blood in which the characters learn about each other's abilities and have a leader selected.

2. Mines Incursion in which the characters defeat a large covert invasion of the mines at Nerr'tenden.

3. The Stoneshapers in which Stoneshaper mages visit Nerr'tenden, and one of them turns out to be an agent.

4. Illiam's Caravan in which the party brings Illiam and Keniryn gold to Llurth Dreier, dead or alive.

5. Orlylyl Family in which Valron's mother orders the Spider Guard to complete the task of the failed Miners Incursion.

For more detailed narrative from Zacxh's perspective, see ZacxhBlog.

Male apprentice bowyer at the House Oussund armory at Nerr'tenden. Of moderate build, fairly attractive, looks comfortable with his weapons.
